| **Tier walk made market-aware (2026-04-26)** | Two-layer fix preventing the "walked into no-market tier" silent-skip pattern diagnosed on the 2026-04-26 slate (LeBron James PTS T15→T10 case: quant qualified at T15 with 75% L20 + T15 vs tough = 86.7%, LLM walked T15→T10 via FG_MARGIN_THIN cascade, FanDuel had no T10 market, `enforce_market_gate()` rejected silently — `[analyst] MARKET_GATE_REJECT: LeBron James PTS T10 — tier not in FanDuel markets (available: [15, 20, 25, 30])` — and the originally-qualifying T15 was lost with no `skipped_picks.json` record). **Layer A** (`agents/analyst.py:build_prompt()` + `build_pick_prompt()` via `replace_all`): added a TIER_WALK MARKET-AWARENESS bullet to the SELECTION RULES section immediately before the existing `pick_value + walked_tier output contract` bullet, instructing the LLM to consult the AVAILABLE FANDUEL MARKETS data already in the prompt before walking down — if the lower tier has no market, keep the pick at the current qualifying tier and apply the step-down's confidence penalty instead. Identical text in both prompts. Scout untouched per project convention (rules-free; doesn't emit walked_tier). **Layer B** (`agents/analyst.py`): new `revert_no_market_walk(picks, player_stats)` post-processor function (~150 lines) inserted between `reconcile_pick_values()` and `filter_self_skip_picks()`. Loads `odds_available.json` via the existing `load_available_markets()` helper; for each pick checks three conditions in sequence — (1) walk-down occurred (`pick_value < best_tiers[prop].tier`), (2) walked tier has no FanDuel market, (3) some tier T in `(walked, best_tier]` has a market AND is in `VALID_TIERS[prop]`. When all three hold, reverts `pick_value` and `walked_tier` to the LOWEST bettable tier in that range (preserves the LLM's safety intent), applies a confidence penalty extracted via local `PENALTY_MAP` regex from `tier_walk` text (FG_MARGIN_THIN -2%, FG_MARGIN_NEG/FG_COLD/VOLATILE/blowout/suppressor/vs_tough -3%, dense_schedule/min_floor/def_recency -2%, default -3% when no keyword recognised), annotates `tier_walk` with `[WALK_REVERTED: T<old>→T<new>, no T<old> market; applied <penalty>% penalty in lieu of step]`, and logs per-pick via `[analyst] WALK_REVERT: ...`. Graceful no-op when `load_available_markets()` returns None (same fail-open posture as the existing market gate). Wired into `save_picks()` chain between `reconcile_pick_values` and `reconcile_game_attribution` (order: tier reconciliation runs first → revert runs against reconciled tiers → home/away reconciles independently → market gate runs last). `save_picks()` signature extended to `save_picks(picks, player_stats: dict | None = None)`; when `player_stats` is None the revert step prints a console line and is skipped (preserves backward compatibility for any test entry point). All 5 production call sites in `main()` updated to pass `player_stats` (which is already loaded at line 5872 via `load_player_stats()`). Either layer alone prevents the LeBron failure; both together provide defense-in-depth identical to the home/away inversion fix architecture from 2026-04-25 (LLM-side rule + Python-side reconciler). **Verification (all gates pass):** Python `ast.parse` clean; spec-grep matrix passes (TIER_WALK MARKET-AWARENESS = 2 in both prompts, AVAILABLE FANDUEL MARKETS section reference = 2, def revert_no_market_walk = 1, call site in save_picks = 1, WALK_REVERT log + annotation refs = 3, PENALTY_MAP local def = 2, signature `save_picks(picks: list[dict], player_stats:` = 1, zero remaining bare `save_picks(picks)` call sites — all 5 updated to `save_picks(picks, player_stats)`, enforce_market_gate / reconcile_pick_values / reconcile_game_attribution definitions all preserved); 5 functional tests pass — (a) canonical LeBron synthetic case reverts T10→T15 with -2% FG_MARGIN_THIN penalty (78→76 confidence), tier_walk annotation correctly appended; (b) non-walked picks (Castle pick=best_tier) pass through unchanged; (c) walked-to-bettable picks (Tatum walked T25→T20 where T20 has market) pass through unchanged; (d) `load_available_markets()` returning None gracefully no-ops; (e) walked-to-no-market with NO bettable higher tier in `(walked, best]` range correctly passes through to let `enforce_market_gate` handle the reject; (f) default -3% penalty applies when no PENALTY_MAP keyword matches. **Empirical motivation:** 2026-04-26 analyst run logs surfaced the LeBron T10 reject; manual review showed T15 was a structurally sound pick (75% L20, 86.7% vs tough, T15 has FanDuel market at 95%+ implied prob). | **Tooling: tools/single_leg_edge_analysis.py — single-leg conf-vs-market delta analysis (2026-04-25)** | New one-off analysis utility. Run: `python -m tools.single_leg_edge_analysis`. Reads `data/picks.json` filtered with the same `is_valid_pick()` predicate as the parlay enumerator (HIT/MISS, voided≠True, market_implied_prob in (0,100), confidence_pct in (0,100), prop_type in {PTS,REB,AST,3PM}). Computes `delta = conf_pct/100 − market_implied_prob/100` per pick, then bins by two systems: (A) data-led deciles via rank-based assignment `decile = min(9, rank * 10 // n)` over delta-sorted records (yields decile sizes within ±1 of n/10), and (B) fixed semantic-tag bands (deep_fade < -0.10 / fade [-0.10, -0.05) / mild_fade [-0.05, 0) / mild_edge [0, 0.05) / medium_edge [0.05, 0.10) / strong_edge ≥ 0.10). Per-prop breakdown for the semantic-tag pass with `n < 15` rows flagged `insufficient_sample` (lower than parlay analysis's n=100 threshold because per-pick analysis on ~400 picks across 4 props × 6 bands inevitably produces small cells). Distribution view: 9-statistic quantile summary (min/p05/p10/p25/p50/p75/p90/p95/max) + histogram with 0.01-wide bins using `math.floor()` for correct negative-value bin assignment (`int()` would truncate toward zero and put -0.073 in the wrong bin). Output: `data/single_leg_edge_report.md` — 7-section markdown report (header+metadata, two verbatim caveat paragraphs about truncated distribution + partial odds coverage, distribution view, decile table, semantic-tag overall table, four per-prop sub-tables, no-commentary footer). **First-run results on 2026-04-25:** 1138 total picks → 348 valid (HIT/MISS, with odds, not voided), 85.6% overall hit rate, date range 2026-03-31 → 2026-04-23 (period since OddsAPI infrastructure shipped 3/31). Decile sizes [35,35,35,35,34,35,35,35,35,34] (target 34.8, max-min=1). Band sizes: deep_fade=262, fade=53, mild_fade=17, mild_edge=11, medium_edge=3, strong_edge=2 — distribution heavily skewed toward FADE side (system is systemically under-confident vs FanDuel's implied probabilities, consistent with H29 finding that the analyst is ~10pp under-confident across all bands at full-season scale). All 8 mathematical invariants pass (sum n by decile = sum n by band = sum n by prop_band = 348; hit_rate == hits/n every cell; mean_delta within [min_delta, max_delta] every decile; decile cardinality 10; band cardinality 6; all 4 props present in by_prop_band). **No interpretive commentary in the report itself; analysis lives in chat.** **Output is a research artifact** — `data/single_leg_edge_report.md` is overwriteable on each run, never read by any production agent. Followup queued in `ROADMAP_active.md`: review report and decide whether conf-vs-market delta should drive analyst filtering, ranking, or be deprecated as decorative. **Companion to the parlay research analysis** — at the parlay level `system_conf` was poorly calibrated (Stable bucket showed +27.8pp delta_vs_system); this script tests whether the underlying single-leg signal is itself predictive at all. Created: `tools/single_leg_edge_analysis.py` (~340 lines), `data/single_leg_edge_report.md` (153 lines). Not touched: any agent file, any ingest script, any workflow file, `tools/parlay_research_*.py`, `tools/parlay_h7_drilldown.py`, `tools/playoff_trajectory_sweep.py`, `data/picks.json` (read-only), `data/parlays.json`, `data/parlay_research_report.md`, `context/nba_season_context.md`. |

| **Parlay Builder widget: market vs calibrated odds calculation (2026-04-23)** | Fixed combined odds calculation in the interactive Parlay Builder widget in `agents/build_site.py` (frontend JS, `renderBuilder()` + `copyBuilder()`). | **Parlay bug fix: find_min_legs_for_bucket sort direction (2026-04-23)** | `find_min_legs_for_bucket()` in `agents/parlay.py` was using descending sort (highest-prob picks first), causing all three odds buckets to be incorrectly skipped on floor-pick-heavy slates. With an 8-leg cap, multiplying the 8 highest-probability picks together (many at 85-97% individual implied prob) still produced ~0.67 combined prob — above the 0.50 Value bucket threshold — so the function returned -1 "unreachable" and every bucket was skipped with "cannot reach +100 within 8 legs" messages. Root cause: to minimize legs required, the LOWEST-prob picks must come first — each leg multiplies the combined probability downward by its own prob, and lower-prob legs descend faster. Fix: function now sorts internally ascending (defensive — safe to pass any order), parameter renamed `legs_sorted` → `picks`, docstring rewritten to explain the reversal. Removed the now-unnecessary `picks_by_prob = sorted(..., reverse=True)` block in `main()` and its 2 comment lines; call site now passes `picks` directly. Production evidence from Apr 23 35-pick slate: pre-fix emitted 0 cards ("Loaded 35 eligible picks … No valid parlay cards generated"). Post-fix: Value reachable at 2 legs (Mobley PTS T15 67.21% × Mitchell AST T4 67.74% = 0.4553 → +120), Standard at 3 legs (0.3130 → +220), Reach at 5 legs (0.1841 → +443) — all three buckets enabled. Scope: `agents/parlay.py` only — single function body + call-site sort removal. `rank_score()`, `build_leg_dict()`, `save_parlays()`, `ODDS_BUCKETS`, `MAX_LEGS`, combo generation loop, all loaders, all workflow files untouched. Verification: 4/4 grep checks pass, Python `ast.parse` clean. |

| **Parlay agent rewrite: combinatorial menu builder (2026-04-22)** | Replaced LLM-based parlay selection (59.8% hit rate, 52/87 despite 85.7% individual pick rate) with a pure-Python combinatorial menu builder. Zero API calls. `agents/parlay.py` full rewrite (1151 → 500 lines). Generates 5-10 ranked cards across three odds buckets: **Value** (+100 to +200, 4 cards), **Standard** (+200 to +350, 3 cards), **Reach** (+350 to +600, 2 cards). **Construction uses `market_implied_prob`** (FanDuel) for odds bucket placement and advertised payout — the actual payout is determined by market odds, not system confidence. **Ranking uses `confidence_pct`** product (`combined_confidence`) — highest system-predicted hit probability wins within each bucket. The two signals are intentionally separated. **Algorithm:** (1) Load today's picks filtered to non-voided, non-skipped, non-OUT/DOUBTFUL, with `market_implied_prob` present (no odds → can't price the parlay). (2) For each bucket, compute minimum legs needed using the highest-probability picks as an optimistic bound (`find_min_legs_for_bucket`). (3) Enumerate `combinations(pool, n)` from min_legs to min_legs+3, filter by no-duplicate-player and bucket prob range, compute `combined_market_prob` and `combined_confidence`, score via composite (confidence × 1000 + n_games × 5 + iron_floor × 3 − n_legs). (4) Early-terminate at 50 candidates per bucket. (5) Rank and select top N per bucket. (6) Global player-appearance cap (`enforce_player_cap`, max 2 cards per player) prevents menu concentration. **Removed:** `load_parlay_audit_feedback()`, `load_cannibalization_data()`, `build_cannibalization_context()`, `get_correlation_tag()`, `score_combination()`, `build_candidates()`, `build_parlay_prompt()`, `call_parlay_agent()`, `enforce_concentration_cap()`, `CORR_BONUS`, `GAME_CONCENTRATION_PENALTY`, all `anthropic`/LLM imports, all `MODEL`/`MAX_TOKENS`/`TOP_N_TO_CLAUDE` config. **Preserved:** path constants, `_norm_team()`, `_extract_last()`, `_load_out_players()`, `load_todays_picks()` (with `market_implied_prob` filter added), `load_todays_picks_review()`, `american_odds()`, `format_odds()`, `save_parlays()` — the `parlays.json` bundle schema is byte-compatible so auditor grading and `build_site.py` rendering work unchanged. **Card schema:** adds `bucket`, `combined_market_prob`, `combined_confidence`, `n_games`, `iron_floor_count`, `rank_score`, `implied_odds_int`; removes `reasoning`, `corr_tags`, `composite_score`, `floor_confidence`, `avg_confidence`, `parlay_type`, `concentration_penalty`. `correlation` field preserved for frontend badge (set from game-count: independent / mixed / positive). **Design rationale:** LLM was actively destroying value — selecting legs correlated on failure modes, over-indexing on narrative coherence. A randomly-constructed 2-leg parlay from the pick pool would hit ~73%. Combinatorial enumeration with game-independence as a ranking bonus, zero narrative bias, and market-priced odds is strictly better. **Auditor unchanged** — it reads `parlays.json` directly for grading; the bundle format is preserved. **No workflow changes** — `analyst.yml` already calls `python agents/parlay.py`. **Verification (7-point spec matrix, all pass):** Python `ast.parse` clean; 0 `import anthropic`; 0 LLM call patterns; `ODDS_BUCKETS` = 3 refs; `market_implied_prob` = 12 refs; `combined_confidence` = 3 refs; `def save_parlays` = 1. `agents/parlay.py` only. |
| **Skip rule recalibration: REB floor 78%→72%, VOLATILE AST T6 softening, PTS/AST grace zone (2026-04-22)** | Three prompt-text changes to `agents/analyst.py` addressing the 91.7% false skip rate observed on 4/21 (11 of 12 skipped picks would have hit) and the ~75% archive-wide FSR. **(1) REB minimum confidence floor lowered from 78% to 72%** — REB has stabilized to 87.6% season hit rate (was the highest-variance category historically; now comparable to PTS) and went 10/10 on the last 10 picks. The 78% floor was over-rejecting: 5 REB picks skipped at 70-77% on Apr 21 all hit. Five REB-related text occurrences updated in lockstep across both `build_prompt()` and `build_pick_prompt()` via `replace_all` (10 total replacements): main rule text, "Both the X% confidence minimum AND floor gate" sentence, tier-walk rule reference, `merit_below_floor` enum comment, and tier-ceiling cross-reference. **(2) VOLATILE + AST T6+ softened for primary playmakers** — was a hard SKIP regardless of player profile. Now bifurcated by `raw_avgs AST ≥ 6.0`: primary playmakers (LeBron, Maxey, Harden, Jokic) get a -8% confidence penalty instead, with the pick proceeding if confidence remains ≥ 70% (else `merit_below_floor`); secondary creators (`<6.0 APG`) continue to receive the hard SKIP. Targets the LeBron AST T6 (7 actual) and Maxey AST T6 (8 actual) false skips. The elite playmaker exemption for the AST T4+ hard gate (≥8.0 APG) is unchanged — this rule governs only the VOLATILE+T6 interaction. **(3) PTS/AST general floor lowered from 70% to 68% (2pp grace zone)** — playoff 70-75% confidence band hits at 89.4%, and picks at 68-69% were systematically over-skipped (Durant PTS at 69% scored 23, Tatum AST at 65% recorded 9). The grace zone recovers near-qualifying picks without quality dilution. The "CONFIDENCE THRESHOLD IS A FLOOR, NOT A TARGET" anti-rounding language was preserved with all numbers updated (68% threshold, 63% honest assessment example). 3PM floor unchanged at 75% — 3PM remains the most volatile prop. **Verified:** 6/6 spec grep checks pass, Python `ast.parse` clean, 3PM 75% references retained (4 occurrences), no top_pick threshold touched. `agents/analyst.py` only — pure prompt text, no Python logic changes. |

| **Opportunity flags OUT player filter fix (2026-04-18)** | `build_opportunity_suggestions()` in `agents/lineup_update.py` was leaking OUT/DOUBTFUL/OFS players into the opportunity-card stream when they had no picks today. Root cause: Source 2 (raw `injuries_today.json`) added Rotowire-abbreviated names like `"l. doncic"` and `"a. reaves"` to the `excluded_players` set, but the comparison against `player_stats` later in the scan loop used full names like `"luka doncic"` and `"austin reaves"` — formats never matched, so the OUT filter quietly passed them through. Source 1 (voided picks, full names) covered any OUT player with a pick today, but Doncic/Reaves had 0 picks and were never voided. Today's failure: Durant's OUT-for-rest absence triggered the LAL opponent scan, surfacing Doncic and Reaves as opportunity candidates. Fix: built a `_team_to_fullnames: dict[str, list[str]]` index from `player_stats` (keyed on `_norm`-normalized team abbrev), then for each Rotowire injury entry resolved the abbreviated name to its full `player_stats` form via last-name + team match. Adds BOTH the raw abbreviated name (backward compat with any other consumer) AND the resolved full name to `excluded_players`. Removed the stale `key == "fetched_at"` early-skip — `_norm("fetched_at")` returns `"FETCHED_AT"` which won't appear in `_team_to_fullnames` so nothing leaks via the metadata key. Verified with synthetic fixture reproducing the Durant/Doncic/Reaves scenario: pre-fix the system would have surfaced both LAL OUT players; post-fix all 3 (Doncic, Reaves, Durant himself as the trigger) are correctly excluded. Backward compat preserved — raw abbreviated names still added so any consumer doing direct injury-name comparisons still works. `agents/lineup_update.py` only. |

| **Rotowire Projected Minutes: Full Coverage Fix — 2026-04-15** | Root cause was an **auth field-name mismatch**, not a page-split (an initial hypothesis based on screenshots of the same page rendering differently for authenticated browsers vs the scraper). `ingest/rotowire_injuries_only.py` `login_rotowire()` sent `data={"username": email, "password": password}` to `https://www.rotowire.com/users/login.php`; the endpoint returned HTTP 200 but granted only a non-premium session cookie, silently gating roughly half the projected-minutes page. Proof: `agents/post_game_reporter.py` uses the same login URL with `data={"email": email, ...}` and authenticates successfully for premium news fetches in production (confirmed working 2026-04-13). Fix: `login_rotowire()` now POSTs with `"email"` as the primary field name, falling back to `"username"` if `email` fails HTTP 200. Between attempts, `session.cookies.clear()` prevents a failed first attempt from poisoning the second. Post-login log shows cookie count + names so production ops logs surface any future auth regression at a glance. **Upstream `parse_projected_minutes()` hardening retained** (added earlier this day when troubleshooting the same bug under the page-split hypothesis): (a) candidate ancestor must contain the literal text `"starters"` (case-insensitive); (b) each player's enclosing `<li>` must contain a digit; (c) post-parse validation requires ≥1 player with `minutes > 0` before accepting a team. These filters are generally-correct hardening even for the dedicated page alone and provide defense-in-depth against future DOM changes. **Earlier same-day workaround reverted:** the dual-parse merge in `main()` (parse both dedicated page and lineups page, merge results) is no longer needed — correctly-authenticated dedicated page serves ALL teams in a single response. `main()` now goes back to the simple single-page parse path, with a new `COVERAGE GAP` log line that surfaces any mismatch between the parsed lineups slate and the teams returned by the projected-minutes page (so the real blocker — if any — stays visible). `agents/rotowire_minutes_diag.py` rewritten as a three-phase investigator: Phase 1 inspects the login page's form fields, Phase 2 runs dual login attempts (email vs username) from fresh sessions and counts teams/players/panels/premium-gate markers on each resulting projected-minutes fetch, Phase 3 prints a side-by-side comparison table with a "VERDICT" line naming the winning field. Writes `data/minutes_diag.json` for archival. **Pre-existing parser bug noted (out-of-scope, unfixed):** the NavigableString section-header detection branch in `parse_projected_minutes()` is dead code (`hasattr(NavigableString, 'name')` returns True in bs4), so every player has always been tagged `section="STARTERS"` in production regardless of source panel — downstream consumers only read the `minutes` value so no downstream impact. Enables PLAYOFF RULE MODIFICATIONS Override 1 (min_floor 84% PTS cap suspension when `projected_minutes ≥ 30`) to fire for all players, not just the ~half previously covered. `ingest/rotowire_injuries_only.py`, `agents/rotowire_minutes_diag.py`. |
| **Playoff Rule Modifications (Layer 1) — 2026-04-15** | Added `build_playoff_rule_modifications()` to `agents/analyst.py` — date-gated to `PLAYOFF_START_DATE` (active for both play-in and playoff games). Three directive overrides active during postseason: (1) MIN_FLOOR confidence cap (PTS 84% when floor_minutes < 24) SUSPENDED when Rotowire `projected_minutes ≥ 30`; (2) VOLATILE confidence deduction reduced from -5% to -3% (iron_floor interaction, VOLATILE+AST T6 skip, weak-combo skip rules unchanged); (3) `team_momentum` tag (hot/cold/neutral) is INFORMATIONAL ONLY — not a confidence modifier. Rationale: regular-season calibration data includes managed rest, DNPs, and low-stakes contests that don't exist in playoffs — the 84% cap understates actual playoff floor, the VOLATILE metric inflates from load-management variance, and regular-season momentum reflects schedule/rest artifacts not predictive of postseason. Block injected in both Scout and Pick prompts directly after `{build_playoff_blowout_override(TODAY_STR)}` and before `KEY RULES — VOLATILITY:`. `build_playoff_context()` "What does NOT change" line updated to remove VOLATILE penalties (no longer accurate) and to forward-reference PLAYOFF RULE MODIFICATIONS. Date-gate verified for 6 dates (pre-gate returns empty, gate day + later returns 2,435-char block). `agents/analyst.py` only. |

| **Spec 5: Skip Re-evaluation Path C — Cannibalization Release (2026-04-11)** | Path C added to `build_skip_reconsiderations()` in `agents/lineup_update.py`: when a skipped player was STRONGLY cannibalized by the absent star (H33 cannib_idx < −15pp), the skip is reconsidered even if Paths A (without-star rate ≥70%) and B (population delta positive) both fail. All data fields (`morning_implied_prob`, `market_implied_prob`, `bet_recommendation.calibrated_prob`) were already being written onto each pick by `ingest/odds_today.py` `main()` (morning) and `pretip_sweep()` (hourly re-fetch) — this task makes them visible on the frontend without any Python, agent, workflow, or ingest changes. Card-face indicator for >3pp moves ("Market agrees ↑" teal or "Market disagrees ↓" amber with prob shift and edge strikethrough); odds drawer shows full detail for all >0.5pp moves. Scope: `agents/build_site.py` only. **Four edits inside `generate_html()`:** (1) **CSS block** after the existing `.edge-line` classes adds `.movement-line` (font-size 10px, margin-top 6px, nowrap, line-height 1.5), `.movement-line.agrees` (teal `#2dd4bf` matching existing POSITIVE edge tier color), `.movement-line.disagrees` (amber `#FF9800` matching existing opportunity-card "no edge" color), `.movement-line.significant` (font-weight 600), `.movement-line .edge-shift` (font-size 9px, opacity 0.8 for the secondary edge-shift span), `.movement-line .edge-shift s` (text-decoration-color inherit + opacity 0.6 for the strikethrough effect), and `.movement-drawer` (font-size 10px, muted color, monospace, line-height 1.6, opacity 0.75 — matches existing `.odds-sizing-body` aesthetic). (2) **New JS function `buildMovementLine(p)`** inserted immediately after `buildEdgeLine()` and before `displayConf()`. Returns empty string on three no-op conditions: `p.voided` (voided picks get no movement indicator regardless of data), `morning_implied_prob == null`, `market_implied_prob == null`. Computes `delta = current - morning` and absolute delta; returns empty string when `absDelta < 3.0` (dead zone for card face — smaller moves go to drawer only). For >3pp moves: `agrees = delta > 0` (market implied probability UP = market agrees with our OVER position), arrow `↑` or `↓`, label "Market agrees" or "Market disagrees", class `agrees` or `disagrees`. Prob shift rendered as rounded integers for compactness (`62→68%`). Edge shift computed from `bet_recommendation.calibrated_prob` when available: `morningEdge = calProb - morning`, `currentEdge = calProb - current`, rendered as a secondary `<span class="edge-shift">edge <s>+X.Xpp</s> → +Y.Ypp</span>` where the strikethrough `<s>` tag marks the stale morning edge. Final return: `<div class="movement-line significant {cls}">{label} {arrow}&nbsp; {probStr}{edgeStr}</div>`. (3) **`buildOddsSizing(p)` drawer extension** — new block inserted AFTER the existing `kelly_quarter` line and BEFORE the `alt_tiers` alt-tier rendering. Shows movement detail for ALL moves >0.5pp (including the 0.5–3pp range that doesn't render on card face). Uses underscore-prefixed local variables (`_morning`, `_current`, `_delta`, `_absDelta`, `_dir`, `_color`, `_mEdge`, `_cEdge`) to avoid any collision with enclosing scope. Gate: `_morning != null && _current != null && _absDelta >= 0.5`. Appends 3 lines unconditionally (`── Line Movement ──` header, directional line with inline color style, morning prob, current prob) plus 2 more conditional lines when `br.calibrated_prob != null` (morning edge, current edge). Directional line uses inline `style="color:{_color}"` so the accent stays consistent with the card-face indicator without needing another CSS class. (4) **Pick card template wiring** — added `${{buildMovementLine(p)}}` line between the existing `${{(function() {{ ... }})()}}` lineup update IIFE and the `${{buildOddsSizing(p)}}` drawer call. Placement is intentional: the movement indicator sits below the lineup-update amendment badge (high-priority contextual alerts) and above the odds drawer toggle (click-to-expand detail), so significant line movement is immediately visible at card-face level before any user interaction. **Thresholds:** card-face ±3pp (significant moves), drawer ±0.5pp (all meaningful moves). The ±3pp card-face threshold is calibrated to avoid noise — FanDuel alternate lines typically tick 0.5–2pp between morning and pretip even with no news; only moves ≥3pp indicate genuine sharp-money repricing or injury-driven shifts. The ±0.5pp drawer threshold captures everything above rounding noise for the user who wants full detail. **Semantic design:** "Market agrees" (teal ↑) means the market's OVER probability moved UP, which agrees with the analyst's OVER pick — but paradoxically the *edge* shrinks because the market is now closer to the system's calibrated probability. "Market disagrees" (amber ↓) means the market's OVER probability moved DOWN, disagreeing with our OVER pick — but the *edge* grows (assuming calibrated_prob is stable). The edge-shift strikethrough visualization makes the dual nature explicit: `edge +5.2 → +2.1pp` (strikethrough on +5.2) when the market agrees and compresses the edge, or `edge -3.1 → +0.8pp` when the market disagrees and widens into our favor. **Voided picks excluded** — even if `morning_implied_prob` and `market_implied_prob` are both populated, `p.voided` short-circuits the function to empty string. **Graceful degradation** — if either prob field is null (pretip didn't run, or pick wasn't matched in morning odds), the function returns empty string and the card renders exactly as before. Same for the drawer block. **Verification (8-point matrix, all pass):** Python `ast.parse` clean on `agents/build_site.py` (pre-existing `\d` SyntaxWarnings unrelated); `function buildMovementLine` count = 1 (definition); `movement-line` count = 7 (CSS + JS class references, well above the ≥4 requirement); `buildMovementLine(p)` count = 2 (function definition line + pick card template call site); `Line Movement` count = 1 (drawer section header); `absDelta < 3.0` = 1 (card-face threshold in `buildMovementLine`); `_absDelta >= 0.5` = 1 (drawer threshold in `buildOddsSizing`); `p.voided) return` ≥1 (voided guard in `buildMovementLine`). **End-to-end build test:** `python3 agents/build_site.py` ran cleanly and produced `site/index.html` (0 today's picks for 4/11 is expected — analyst hasn't run yet today, and no pretip data has been written to any pick for 4/11). **Untouched:** `buildEdgeLine()` function (unchanged, still shows current-edge badge based on `bet_recommendation.recommendation_tier`), `buildOddsSizing()` existing lines up through `kelly_quarter` (only the new block after kelly_quarter was added), all other JS functions (`displayConf`, `buildMicroStats`, `buildHitRate`, `toggleOddsSizing`, `toggleTierWalk`, `toggleLineupUpdate`, `renderPicks`, `renderBestBets`, `renderTopPicks`, `renderParlays`, `renderResults`, `renderAudit`, `renderResearch`, `renderPlayoffProfiles`, `renderPlayoffExplorer`, `renderCurrentSeasonExplorer`), Python code in `build_site.py` (all `build_*` data preparation functions, `get_top_picks`, `load_*` loaders, `main()` / `build_site()` entry point), `agents/analyst.py`, `agents/auditor.py`, `agents/quant.py`, `agents/parlay.py`, `agents/lineup_watch.py`, `agents/lineup_update.py`, `ingest/odds_today.py`, all `.yml` workflow files, `picks.json` schema (purely a frontend-visibility change reading fields that were already present). `agents/build_site.py` only. |

| **H26 Star-Absence Uplift Annotation — Part 1 of 2 (2026-04-11)** | Per-player star-absence lift data added to `agents/quant.py` + corresponding annotation block in `agents/analyst.py` `build_quant_context()`. Two-line output when `sal["star_name"]` is in `_out_set`: (1) population reference `STAR_ABSENT_LIFT: [<star> OUT] population PTS T15-T25 +11 to +13pp, AST T4 +10pp`; (2) per-player line `Player-specific (Ng): <best_tier_key> delta +Xpp [<qualifier>]` showing the highest-delta key tier from `key_deltas`. PERSONAL_DRAG_WARNING case adds " — population lift does NOT apply to this player". POPULATION_ONLY case shows `Player-specific: <3 without-star games [POPULATION_ONLY]`. Hardcoded `3` for SA_MIN_CONDITION_N to avoid cross-module import coupling (documented in inline comment). **Part 2B wiring** — `star_lift_line` added to the `lines.append(...)` block between `kta_line` and `opp_absence_str`. **Part 2C qualifier reference** — added to TWO prompt rules: (a) `build_prompt()` `WITHOUT-STAR BASELINE — TWO REQUIRED GATES` block (line ~2095) — new paragraph after the intro explaining that STAR_ABSENT_LIFT is informational and does NOT override the two gates, with explicit per-qualifier rules (PERSONAL_DRAG_WARNING → do NOT apply population lift, STRONG_PERSONAL_SIGNAL → factor positively, POPULATION_ONLY → directional only, NEUTRAL → no lift). (b) `build_pick_prompt()` `KEY RULES — TEAMMATE ABSENCE USAGE ABSORPTION` block — same semantic paragraph with wording adapted to the Pick prompt's existing style (Pick prompt uses TEAMMATE ABSENCE USAGE ABSORPTION instead of the WITHOUT-STAR BASELINE TWO GATES framing). | **Skip Rule Refinements — 4 edits (2026-04-11)** | Four surgical prompt-text edits to `agents/analyst.py` correcting high-false-skip-rate rules and aligning the monolithic `build_prompt()` with the H19-relaxed `build_pick_prompt()`. No Python logic changes, no schema changes, no new `skip_reason` enum values. All edits applied to BOTH `build_prompt()` and `build_pick_prompt()` (Scout prompt untouched — rules-free by design), except Edit D which was monolithic-only because Pick was already correct. **Motivation:** audit_summary.json showed `blowout_t25_skip` 100% FSR (2/2 — Maxey actual 32, Wembanyama actual 40), `blowout_secondary_scorer` 100% FSR (2/2), `3pm_blowout_trend_down` 66.7% FSR (2/3), and the H27 backtest (Apr 11, n=68 primary scorers at spread_abs ≥ 15) confirmed primary scorer PTS T25 hit rate at 58.8% — MARGINAL vs 50.6% baseline, NOT SUPPRESSED. **Edit A — `blowout_t25_skip` elite scorer exemption:** Two hunks in BOTH prompts, both applied via `replace_all=true` since the source text was byte-identical. (1) TIER CEILING RULES `PTS T25 BLOWOUT HARD SKIP` block rewritten to add an `EXCEPTION — elite scorers` clause: players with `raw_avgs PTS >= 27.0` are exempt from the hard skip and proceed through normal T25 evaluation, where the 80% hit rate bar (8+/10) still applies and the existing `spread_abs >= 15` confidence cap (74% max) still constrains the pick. Non-elite scorers (raw_avgs PTS < 27.0) remain hard-skipped. Rationale cites H27: population T25 hit rate at 58.8% is below floor, but elite scorers with 8+/10 individual rates significantly outperform population. (2) ELITE SCORER BLOWOUT EXEMPTION "Exception to the exemption" paragraph rewritten: the `spread_abs >= 15` cap still applies universally, but the note now clarifies that PTS T25 for elite scorers (raw_avgs PTS >= 27.0) is NOT hard-skipped — it proceeds through normal T25 eval at the 74% cap. Non-elite scorers remain hard-skipped. The two hunks are self-consistent and cross-reference each other. **Edit B — `blowout_secondary_scorer` threshold lowered + co-primary gate + T10 floor exception:** Applied separately in each prompt because the source texts differed (build_prompt had the stale pre-H19 `spread_abs > 8` version, build_pick_prompt had the H19-relaxed `spread_abs ≥ 15` version). Final replacement identical in both: (a) threshold lowered to `spread_abs >= 13.5` (between H19's 15 and the original > 8 — splits the difference where blowout is near-certain but not extreme); (b) new `T10 FLOOR EXCEPTION` clause — the skip does NOT apply when pick tier is T10 PTS, because T10 is the system's minimum PTS tier with near-certain population hit rates and the minute-compression risk is adequately handled by existing `min_floor` rules; (c) new `CO-PRIMARY SCORER GATE` — a player with `raw_avgs PTS >= 22.0` is always classified as PRIMARY regardless of teammate tier comparison, preventing the rule from firing against one of two co-primary scorers (example in text: Fox ~25 PPG and Wembanyama ~24 PPG are both above 22.0 → both primaries, rule fires for neither); (d) at `spread_abs 8–13`, apply the standard BLOWOUT_RISK confidence penalty (-10 to -15pp) INSTEAD of a hard skip — this is the H19 finding (n=140, lift=1.083 at 8–14 spread_abs) extended to the 13 cutoff. The pre-existing PRIMARY/SECONDARY tiebreaker text (based on best qualifying PTS tier) is retained as the fallback when the co-primary gate doesn't apply (i.e. when neither player is above 22.0 PPG). **Edit C — 3PM trend=down T1 iron_floor exception:** Applied to BOTH prompts via `replace_all=true` (identical source text). The unconditional T1 step-down skip now has an exception: if the player has `iron_floor` on 3PM OR a 9+/10 hit rate at T1, hold at T1 (do NOT skip) and apply a -5% confidence penalty to reflect the declining trend. Rationale: iron_floor or 9+/10 at T1 confirms a structural floor of 1+ make per game; the declining trend is real signal warranting a confidence deduction, but does not justify eliminating a near-certain prop. Fox 3PM T1 (actual 2) and Wembanyama 3PM T1 (actual 2) were both false-skipped by the unconditional T1 step-down on 2026-04-10. The exception applies ONLY to the trend=down step-down from T1 — the trend=down + tough DvP hard skip and the trend=down + limited minutes hard skip still override it when their conditions are met. **Edit D — Align monolithic build_prompt() 3PM blowout rule with H19:** The monolithic prompt had the stale pre-H19 `3PM hard skip — trend=down AND blowout_risk=True` block (hard-skipping all 3PM at `spread_abs > 8` on the favored side) while `build_pick_prompt()` was correctly updated by the H19 backtest (2026-03-22) to use step-down-only at `spread_abs 8–18`. Rewrote the monolithic block to match the Pick prompt's H19-aligned version: at `spread_abs 8–18` apply the existing trend=down step-down rule only (no hard skip); at `spread_abs >= 19` the unconditional extreme-blowout hard skip (pre-existing) still fires. The step-down now benefits from Edit C's T1 iron_floor exception for players who reach T1 via the step. The `build_pick_prompt()` version was explicitly NOT touched in this edit — it was already correct. Rationale cites H19 backtest (n=96–137) where blowout_win 3PM hits at 78.8–79.2% (lift=1.097–1.103), above the 71.8% baseline — the hard skip was blocking a high-hit-rate population. **Interaction with existing rules:** All four edits are annotation-only prompt text refinements. No new `skip_reason` enum values added or removed — the existing `blowout_t25_skip`, `blowout_secondary_scorer`, `3pm_blowout_trend_down` remain unchanged. `blowout_secondary_scorer` occurrence count in `analyst.py` = 8 (unchanged). No Python post-processors modified. No schema changes. The ROAD UNDERDOG NEAR-THRESHOLD PTS PENALTY rule immediately following the secondary scorer block is untouched in both prompts. **Verification (10-point spec grep matrix, all pass):** (1) Python `ast.parse` clean; (2) `EXCEPTION — elite scorers: Players with raw_avgs PTS >= 27.0` present exactly 2× (one per prompt function); (3) `spread_abs >= 13.5` present 4× (header + "At spread_abs >= 13.5 the blowout is near-certain" + T10 exception per prompt × 2 prompts = 4); (4) old `BLOWOUT_RISK SECONDARY SCORER SKIP.*spread_abs.*15` pattern = 0 (fully removed); (5) `CO-PRIMARY SCORER GATE` present 2×; (6) `T10 FLOOR EXCEPTION` present 2×; (7) `iron_floor on 3PM OR a 9+/10` present 2×; (8) old `3PM hard skip — trend=down AND blowout_risk=True` header = 0 (monolithic fully aligned); (9) new `3PM trend=down in blowout context (spread_abs 8–18)` header present 2× (both prompts now aligned); (10) `SECONDARY SCORER SKIP.*spread_abs > 8` = 0 (no stale `> 8` text remaining); (11) `blowout_secondary_scorer` enum count = 8 unchanged. Both `3PM hard skip — extreme blowout` headers (`spread_abs >= 19` in monolithic, `spread_abs ≥ 19` in Pick — Pick keeps its original unicode form since it wasn't touched) are preserved exactly as they were. **Not touched** per spec: `build_scout_prompt()` (rules-free by design), `build_review_prompt()`, `agents/auditor.py`, `agents/parlay.py`, `agents/backtest.py`, `agents/quant.py`, `agents/build_site.py`, `agents/lineup_watch.py`, `agents/lineup_update.py`, all `ingest/*.py`, all `.yml` workflow files, `context/nba_season_context.md`, skip_reason enum values, skip_reason documentation lines in OUTPUT FORMAT blocks, JSON output format, Python post-processors (`filter_self_skip_picks`, `reconcile_pick_values`, `enforce_market_gate`). `agents/analyst.py` only — 7 Edit calls total (2 via `replace_all=true`, 5 unique-context). |

New function `run_series_progression_analysis(args)` in 7 steps: (1) load `playoff_career_log.csv`, filter `season_type == "playoff"` and `minutes > 0`; (2) infer series via sorted team-pair matchup_str, sort by (season, matchup_str, player_name, game_date), assign `game_in_series` per player via `cumcount() + 1`, derive `series_phase` (early G1-2, mid G3-4, late G5+), compute `series_length` per (season, matchup, player) group; (3) population-level phase analysis computing per-stat per-tier per-phase pooled hit rates + avg_stat + avg_minutes + early_to_late_delta_pp; (4) per-player iteration with ≥15 playoff games gate, compute per-phase hit rates at key tier with ≥5-game phase floor, progression_delta_pp (late − early) only when both phases qualify, per-stat flag (LATE_RISER ≥+8pp, LATE_FADER ≤-8pp, STABLE, None when insufficient), full `all_tiers` detail per stat for every tier/phase combo that meets the floor; (5) per-series game logs grouped by (season, matchup_str) with per-game pts/reb/ast/tpm/minutes + game_num + phase, sorted by date within each series and chronologically across series; (5b) overall player flag driven by PTS flag with cross-stat fallback; (6) stdout report with population table (4 stats × 3-4 tiers × 3 phases + early→late delta column), grouped per-player tables (LATE_RISERS sorted by PTS delta desc, STABLE by max_abs_delta, LATE_FADERS by |PTS delta| desc, INSUFFICIENT_DATA), sample size warning note; (7) JSON write with `metadata` (constants, flag_counts), `population` (pooled rates with early_to_late_delta_pp per tier), `players` (sorted entries with full series_log arrays), `summary` (name lists per flag). | **Backtest: H30 minutes elasticity (2026-04-11)** | New `--mode minutes-elasticity` added to `agents/backtest.py`. Quantifies each player's production-vs-minutes curve across 4 absolute minutes buckets to identify who benefits most from the structural minutes increase in playoff basketball. Uses `player_game_log.csv` only (via existing `load_player_log()`). **Implementation** (`agents/backtest.py` only): new constants `H30_STATS`, `H30_STAT_COL`, `H30_TIERS` (PTS 15/20/25/30, REB 4/6/8/10, AST 2/4/6/8, 3PM 1/2/3), `H30_KEY_TIER` (PTS T20, REB T6, AST T4, 3PM T2), `H30_MIN_BUCKET_N=5`, `H30_MIN_TOTAL_GAMES=20`, `H30_MINUTES_BINS=[0,30,34,38,60]`, `H30_MINUTES_LABELS=["low","normal","high","extended"]`, `H30_SCALES_THRESHOLD=10.0`, `H30_INVERTS_THRESHOLD=-10.0`, `H30_POPULATION_MIN_MIN=28` (for starter-level population pool), `MINUTES_ELASTICITY_JSON`. New function `run_minutes_elasticity_analysis(player_log, args)` in 6 steps: (1) copy player_log, coerce `minutes_raw` to numeric, drop zero-minute rows, bucket via `pd.cut` with `right=False` so boundaries are [0,30)/[30,34)/[34,38)/[38,60); (2) per-player iteration with minimum-games gate (≥20), compute per-stat per-tier per-bucket hit rates (cells with n<5 excluded from output), avg_stat per bucket, `bucket_counts` covering all 4 buckets; (3) elasticity delta at the key tier = (extended − normal) × 100, per-stat flag (SCALES/PLATEAUS/INVERTS), monotonicity check (all rates non-decreasing from low→extended across buckets with ≥5 games), overall player flag: MINUTES_SCALER (PTS SCALES), SELECTIVE_SCALER (PTS PLATEAUS + other stat SCALES), MIXED (PTS PLATEAUS + 1+ INVERTS), MINUTES_INDEPENDENT (all PLATEAUS), MINUTES_INVERTER (PTS INVERTS), INSUFFICIENT_DATA (elasticity unavailable); (3b) playoff_projection sub-object includes `extended_key_rates` and `vs_overall_delta` per stat; (4) population aggregation pooled across starter-level players (avg min ≥ 28), per-stat per-tier bucket rates + population elasticity; (5) stdout report with population table (4 stats × 3–4 tiers × 4 buckets + elasticity column), grouped per-player tables (SCALERS / SELECTIVE_SCALERS / MIXED / INDEPENDENT / INVERTERS / INSUFFICIENT_DATA) showing avg_min / n_ext / PTS(T20) low→norm→high→ext progression string (with `—` for excluded buckets) / elasticity / monotonic marker (↑ / · / ?) / flag; (6) JSON write with `metadata` (date, constants, flag_counts), `population` (pooled bucket rates + elasticity per tier), `players` (sorted by PTS elasticity descending with full tier/bucket detail + monotonic flags + playoff_projection), `summary` (name lists per flag category). Wired `--mode minutes-elasticity` dispatch in `main()` after `primary-blowout` (uses standard `player_log` loader). `--mode` help extended. **Production run result (3,533 non-DNP games, 58 unique players, 56 qualified at ≥20 games, 49 starter-level for population pool):** **Population elasticity is massive and monotonically increasing** at every PTS/REB/AST tier. Key results: PTS T15 +16.1pp, PTS T20 +26.0pp, PTS T25 +28.9pp, PTS T30 +26.6pp, REB T6 +17.0pp, AST T4 +21.1pp, AST T6 +26.7pp, 3PM T2 +9.6pp. 3PM is shot-allocation-bound not minutes-bound. **Flag small-sample, directionally consistent with age/efficiency narratives but not definitive), 22 INSUFFICIENT_DATA (players whose avg minutes sits below ~32 so they don't log ≥5 games at 38+). | **Pretip sweep: closing-line re-fetch architecture (2026-04-11)** | Replaces the "fetch once, dedup forever" model in `pretip_sweep()` step 4 with a "re-fetch when closer to tip-off" model. Under the old model, each game was fetched at most once per day — whichever hourly sweep first hit the game's window captured its odds. This produced noisy CLV data because a line captured 3–5 hours before tip doesn't reflect the market's final assessment; sharp-money movement, injury news, and lineup confirmations all happen in the last 1–2 hours. New model: each sweep re-fetches a game when `(prior_minutes_to_tip − current_minutes_to_tip) >= CLOSING_LINE_MIN_IMPROVEMENT` (30 min). Commenced games (`minutes_to_tip < 0`) are locked — no re-fetch, no credit burn. Combined with the tip-off guard shipped earlier today, the last successful pre-tip fetch becomes the definitive closing line. **Implementation** (`ingest/odds_today.py` only): (1) New constant `CLOSING_LINE_MIN_IMPROVEMENT = 30` near `PRETIP_GRACE_MINUTES`; the 30-min floor prevents marginal re-fetches from wasting credits on cron jitter (e.g., two GitHub Actions runs 5 min apart). With hourly cron the typical improvement is ~60 min so every run qualifies. (2) Step 4 dedup block replaced entirely. Old code built `already_fetched` set from `pretip_data.snapshots` keys and filtered to only unfetched events. New code iterates `in_window_events` and classifies each as: first-fetch (no prior snapshot → include), commenced (`current_mtt < 0` → skip with `n_skip_commenced += 1`), missing prior mtt (legacy snapshot → re-fetch defensively with `n_refetch += 1`), significant improvement (`prior_mtt − current_mtt >= 30` → re-fetch with `n_refetch += 1`), or marginal (skip with `n_skip_marginal += 1`). Status print line shows the per-bucket counts (e.g. `Closing-line filter: 7 re-fetch (closer to tip), 1 commenced (locked), 1 first capture`). (3) Step 5 fetch log updated to distinguish first-fetch from re-fetch — when `prior_snapshots.get(event_id)` has a `minutes_to_tip`, logs `Re-fetched: AWAY @ HOME (was +Nmin, now +Mmin to tip)` showing the improvement; otherwise logs the original `Fetched: AWAY @ HOME (tips in N min)` line. **Untouched:** snapshot save path (`pretip_data.setdefault("snapshots", {})[event_id] = {...}` already overwrites by event_id, so re-fetched games naturally replace their prior snapshot — only the closest-to-tip capture is preserved); step 6 annotation loop (picks get `market_implied_prob` overwritten with latest odds, morning guard preserved, tip-off guard preserved); `compute_edge()` (runs after annotation, recalculates calibrated edge against the latest market price); `_write_pretip_file()` + picks.json write; `PRETIP_GRACE_MINUTES`; `main()` morning annotation; `save_morning_baseline()`. **Credit budget** (paid tier, 20k credits/month): ~20–28 credits/game/day (5–7 hourly fetches × 4 credits for 4 alternate markets) vs 4 credits/game/day under old model. For a 10-game slate: ~200–280 credits/day, well within budget. **Unit tests** (9 total): (1) synthetic 8-sweep walkthrough matching the spec's table — Game A tips 4:30 PM, Game B tips 7:00 PM: Game A gets 5 fetches (12/1/2/3/4 PM) → 20 credits, locked at 5 PM when commenced; Game B gets 8 fetches (12/1/2/3/4/5/6/7 PM) → 32 credits, closing line captured at +0 min (right at tip); total = 52 credits for 2 games, matching spec arithmetic. (2–7) edge cases: 5-min improvement → skip (marginal); exactly 30-min improvement → fetch (threshold is `>=`); first fetch → `n_refetch` not incremented; legacy snapshot missing `minutes_to_tip` → defensive re-fetch; `mtt=0` (right at tip) → fetch (not yet commenced); `mtt=-5` (commenced) → locked. All 6 edge cases pass. **Verification:** `grep -c "already_fetched" ingest/odds_today.py` = 0 (old dedup set fully removed); `grep -n "CLOSING_LINE_MIN_IMPROVEMENT\|re-fetch\|Re-fetched\|Closing-line\|n_refetch\|improvement\|marginal" ingest/odds_today.py` shows 19 references covering the constant, classification logic, counters, status print, and Re-fetched log line. Python `ast.parse` clean. `ingest/odds_today.py` only — no workflow, agent, or schema changes. |
| **Pretip sweep: tip-off guard on market_implied_prob (2026-04-11)** | Prevents `pretip_sweep()` in `ingest/odds_today.py` from overwriting `market_implied_prob` on picks whose game has already started. On 2026-04-10, MIN@HOU was fetched at `minutes_to_tip=-29` (29 min AFTER tip-off) because the 30-minute `PRETIP_GRACE_MINUTES` grace window allows post-tip fetches for dedup/snapshot purposes. The spec contract is that `market_implied_prob` must be a pre-game closing line for CLV integrity — Amen Thompson's AST T4 price was overwritten from 81.13 (pre-game) to 81.82 (potentially live), contaminating CLV. Root cause: step 6 (the pick annotation loop) had no tip-off awareness — it used the same `fetched` dict regardless of whether each event was pre- or post-tip. **Fix:** two-part change in `pretip_sweep()` only. (1) After `in_window_events` construction and the window summary print, a new `commenced_teams: set[str]` is built by iterating `in_window_events` for any entry with `minutes_to_tip < 0` and adding both `home_abbr` and `away_abbr` to the set. Log line `[odds-pretip] Commenced teams (live line guard active): ...` fires when non-empty. Placed BEFORE the early-empty-exit and BEFORE the dedup step so it reflects the full in-window population, not just the to-fetch subset. (2) In the step 6 annotation loop, immediately after the match lookup (`match = fetched.get(...)`) and before the morning-implied capture, a tip-off guard block checks `pick.get("team")` and `pick.get("opponent")` against `commenced_teams`. If either team has commenced AND the pick already has a `market_implied_prob` value, `continue` — preserving the pre-game price. If the game has commenced but the pick has no prior price (edge case: morning annotation missed this pick), a WARNING is logged and the post-tip line is allowed through — having *some* price, even live, is better than null for `compute_edge()`, but the warning flags it as CLV-unreliable. **Key behaviors preserved:** Phase 1 (fetch/dedup/snapshot) is completely unchanged. `PRETIP_GRACE_MINUTES` still allows post-tip fetches — snapshots are still written to `odds_pretip.json` so future runs correctly dedup on event_id. Only the pick annotation in step 6 is guarded. **CLV semantics:** for picks whose game commences before a clean pretip capture, CLV now degrades to 0 (morning = market, no movement) instead of being contaminated — which is correct: missing movement is not the same as negative movement. **Unit test** (synthetic 4-pick walkthrough matching the 4/10 HOU incident): `commenced_teams = {HOU, MIN}` from one event at `minutes_to_tip=-29`; Amen Thompson HOU (`market_implied_prob=81.13`) and Sengun HOU (`97.22`) both hit the skip branch and preserve their pre-game prices; Cade Cunningham DET @ CHA (`minutes_to_tip=+204`) is NOT in `commenced_teams` and proceeds to normal overwrite; a synthetic Ghost player with `market_implied_prob=None` on the commenced HOU game triggers the WARNING log and allows the first-capture overwrite. All 4 assertions pass. `grep -n "commenced_teams\|tip-off guard\|post-tip" ingest/odds_today.py` shows 5 `commenced_teams` refs + the guard comment + the WARNING log line. Python `ast.parse` clean. **Not touched** per spec: `PRETIP_GRACE_MINUTES` constant, the fetch/dedup logic in steps 1–5, `morning_implied_prob` handling (set-once guard unchanged), `main()` (morning annotation — always pre-tip by design), `compute_edge()`, `save_morning_baseline()`, `_write_pretip_file()`. `ingest/odds_today.py` only. |
| **Opportunity Flags: Odds Enrichment for Tier Cards (2026-04-11)** | Adds FanDuel market implied probability to opportunity-flag tier entries so users can see betting edge at a glance on each opportunity card. Motivated by the 2026-04-10 odds landscape where 67% of picks were FADE (negative calibrated edge) — knowing the market price next to the quant hit rate is critical context when evaluating a late-scratch opportunity. Two-file change, purely additive (no behavioral changes for consumers that don't read the new fields). **File 1 — `agents/lineup_update.py`:** (1) New module path constant `ODDS_AVAILABLE_JSON = DATA / "odds_available.json"` placed next to the existing `INJURIES_JSON` / `MASTER_CSV` constants. (2) New helper `_norm_odds_name(name)` immediately after `_norm()`; strips all punctuation with `re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9 ]", "", name.lower()).strip()` to match the normalization used by `ingest/odds_today.py` (lowercase, collapse hyphens/apostrophes/periods). `re` imported inline inside the helper so the module-level imports are untouched. Deliberately DIFFERENT from `_norm()` which handles team abbreviations — both helpers coexist without collision. (3) New odds-loading block inside `build_opportunity_suggestions()` placed after the `excluded_players` construction and before the `# Morning spread from player_stats` comment. Reads `odds_available.json`, validates `date == TODAY_STR`, extracts the `players` dict into `odds_players: dict`. Graceful no-op on any failure path (missing file, stale date, JSON parse error, any exception) — logs a diagnostic line and proceeds with `odds_players = {}` so the rest of the function is unaffected. (4) Tier enrichment inside the per-prop scanning loop, placed immediately after the existing `tier_entry` dict construction and the `without_player_*` annotation. For each candidate `(teammate_name, prop, tier)` triple: normalize the teammate name via `_norm_odds_name()`, look up `odds_players.get(odds_key, {})`, walk the `prop_odds` list for an entry with matching `tier`, and copy `implied_prob` and `odds` onto the tier_entry as `market_implied_pct` and `market_odds`. Both fields are optional — the tier_entry dict remains valid with or without them. Covers both the qualifying_tiers path (new picks) and the upgrade_tiers path (both share the same `tier_entry` reference). **File 2 — `agents/build_site.py`:** (1) `qtLines` template (opportunity card qualifying-tier rows) extended with a market-price span that renders when `info.market_implied_pct` is present. Format: `(mkt N%)` at font-size 10px, color coded green (`#4CAF50`) when `market_implied_pct <= hit_rate_pct` (system has edge) or orange (`#FF9800`) otherwise (market is more confident than the quant data — no edge). Rounded to integer percent for display. Appended to the existing hr/whr span so the row reads `STAT Ttier  HR% · whr (mkt N%)`. (2) `utLines` template (upgrade-tier rows) given the same treatment with the `(mkt N%)` span appended after the existing `(upgrade)` label. Both templates use f-string double-brace escaping (`{{` / `}}`) because the JS is inside a Python f-string. **Graceful degradation paths:** (a) If `odds_available.json` is missing or stale, `odds_players = {}` and no tier_entry gains market fields → frontend renders exactly as before. (b) If a specific player is in the odds file but the requested tier isn't offered by FanDuel, the tier_entry gets no market fields → that row renders without the `(mkt N%)` span. (c) If `market_implied_pct` is `null` or `undefined`, the JS guard `(info.market_implied_pct !== undefined && info.market_implied_pct !== null)` returns empty string → no span. (d) `market_odds` is copied but currently unused in the display; available for future UI expansion. **Verification:** `grep` confirms constant, helper, load block, enrichment, and template updates are all present. Python `ast.parse` clean on both files. Standalone unit test against real `data/odds_available.json` (137 players, 2026-04-10): (a) `_norm_odds_name` produces correct output for all 5 previously-broken hyphen/apostrophe/period cases (`karlanthony towns`, `deaaron fox`, `cj mccollum`, `jabari smith jr`, matching the fix pattern established in the 2026-04-09 player name normalization bug); (b) 5 of 6 test names match real file keys (SGA missing because OKC isn't playing today — expected, not a bug); (c) synthetic enrichment path successfully looks up Jaylen Brown PTS T20 → `mkt=88.89% odds=-800` and PTS T15 → `mkt=98.36% odds=-6000`; (d) no-market graceful path (Ghost Player) leaves tier_entry untouched — `market_implied_pct` correctly absent; (e) color logic unit test confirms all 5 edge/no-edge scenarios render the correct color (green when mkt ≤ hit, orange when mkt > hit). **Not touched** per spec: `opportunity_flags.json` schema (additive fields only, legacy consumers unaffected), `save_opportunity_flags()`, `compute_lineup_diff()`, dedup key, card_type logic, the opportunity card's left-column player/trigger rendering, all pick-card rendering outside the two template functions. | **Opportunity flags: filter OUT/DOUBTFUL players (2026-04-11)** | Fixes a bug in `build_opportunity_suggestions()` in `agents/lineup_update.py` where players themselves listed OUT, DOUBTFUL, or OFS were being surfaced as late-scratch opportunities. Default `None` preserves backward compatibility — if a caller doesn't pass injuries, the filter is a no-op (same behavior as before). (2) New `excluded_players: set[str]` built near the top of the function, right after the `absence_changes` early return.
