| **Analyst: JSON integrity instructions for Scout/Pick/Review prompts (2026-04-11)** | Adds a closing JSON-integrity instruction to the OUTPUT FORMAT section of all four prompt builders in `agents/analyst.py`. Root cause: on 2026-04-10, all three agent calls (Scout, Pick, Review) required `json_repair` fallback on the same run because Claude produced malformed JSON — trailing commas, unterminated strings, and at least one unbalanced brace. The `json_repair` fallback caught these, but the failure rate is high enough to justify a prompt-side mitigation. **Implementation:** identical instruction inserted into four locations: (1) `build_prompt()` (Pick v1, single-call fallback mode) — before the closing `"""`, after the final `skips rules` bullet; (2) `build_scout_prompt()` — after the shortlist JSON schema closing brace, before the closing `"""`; (3) `build_pick_prompt()` (Pick v2, scout+pick mode) — after the final `skips rules` bullet, before `## AUDITOR FEEDBACK FROM PREVIOUS DAYS`; (4) `build_review_prompt()` — after the "After the closing ] you may add a brief note" line, before the closing `"""`. Instruction text (identical in all 4): `"CRITICAL: Verify your JSON is well-formed before stopping. Every opening {{ must have a matching }}. Every opening [ must have a matching ]. Every string must be closed with a matching quote. Do not emit a trailing comma after the last element in any array or object."` The `{{` / `}}` in the source render as literal `{` / `}` in the final prompt (single-level f-string escaping — all four prompts are `return f"""..."""` without nested interpolation). **Deviation from spec:** the task spec suggested using `{{{{` / `}}}}` (4-char) in the Pick v2 and Review inserts because the surrounding schemas use that convention. Empirical test showed 4-char `{{{{` renders as `{{` (two literal braces) in all four prompts, which would produce an incoherent instruction ("Every opening `{{` must have a matching `}}`"). Used `{{` / `}}` (2-char, renders as `{` / `}`) in all four inserts so the instruction describes actual JSON syntax. Rendered all four prompts with dummy args and confirmed each contains the literal text `"Every opening { must have a matching }. Every opening [ must have a matching ]."`. Pre-existing `{{{{` quirk in the Scout, Pick v2, and Review schema examples (which renders JSON schema with `{{` instead of `{`) is unrelated to this task and was not touched — the spec explicitly forbids modifying schema definitions, and Claude has been correctly interpreting the double-brace schema as single-brace JSON in production. The `json_repair` fallback in `call_scout()`, `call_analyst()`, and `call_review()` is retained as a safety net. Verification: `grep -c "Verify your JSON is well-formed" agents/analyst.py` = 4; Python parse clean; all four prompts render the instruction with literal `{` and `}` characters at offsets 70267, 5153, 68419, 6239 respectively. `agents/analyst.py` only — four string insertions, no logic changes. |
| **Analyst: review file staleness check on re-run (2026-04-11)** | Fixes a bug in `apply_review_flags()` in `agents/analyst.py` where same-day analyst re-runs with different pick sets were blocked from writing fresh `picks_review_YYYY-MM-DD.json` files. Root cause: the existence guard at line 4085 treated ANY existing review file as manual (Oliver-written), so same-day re-runs (e.g. after the Scout 4096→12288 token fix on 4/10 that expanded the shortlist from 8 to 30+ players) would find the old auto-generated file and return without writing. Downstream effect on 4/10: 18 new picks from the expanded Scout shortlist had no review coverage, and `build_site.py` rendered them without any review badges. **Implementation:** replaced the simple `if review_path.exists(): return` block with a staleness-aware guard that inspects the existing file's contents. (1) Load the existing file (or treat as empty on JSON parse error); (2) compute `has_manual = any(e.get("source") != "auto" for e in existing_review)` — if ANY entry lacks the `source: "auto"` marker (including mixed auto+manual files), treat the file as manual and return without overwriting; (3) otherwise compute set-difference between the current pick keys `(name.lower(), prop_type, pick_value)` and the existing review keys; (4) if `current - existing` is empty, the existing auto file covers all current picks → skip regeneration (no unnecessary API-burn); (5) otherwise the file is stale → log `"picks_review file is STALE — covers N picks but current run has M (K uncovered). Regenerating."` and fall through to the existing verdict-mapping and write logic. Docstring updated to document the four guard paths (manual never-overwrite, covers-all skip, stale regenerate, missing regenerate). **Key behaviors preserved:** manual review files (any entry without `source: "auto"`) are NEVER overwritten — identical to current behavior. Auto files with complete coverage are never regenerated unnecessarily. **Key behavior changed:** auto files that are stale relative to the current pick set are now regenerated instead of silently skipped. **Unit tests (6 scenarios):** (a) No existing file → `no-file` → regenerate ✓; (b) Existing manual file → `manual` → skip (never overwrite) ✓; (c) Mixed auto+manual file → `manual` → skip (any non-auto entry wins) ✓; (d) Auto file covers all current picks → `covers-all` → skip (no API burn) ✓; (e) **Auto file STALE (4/10 re-run bug case)** — 15-pick auto file vs 33-pick current run → `stale` (18 new picks uncovered) → regenerate ✓; (f) Empty auto file `[]` + picks present → `stale` → regenerate ✓; (g) Corrupt JSON file → treated as empty → `stale` → regenerate ✓. All 6 pass. `agents/analyst.py` only (only the `apply_review_flags()` guard block + its docstring). Untouched: `build_review_context()`, `build_review_prompt()`, `call_review()`, the verdict mapping, the write logic, `main()` call site, `build_site.py` review-badge rendering, the `picks_review_YYYY-MM-DD.json` schema. |
| **picks.json cross-workflow merge guard for injuries.yml (2026-04-10)** | Prevents the race condition where an in-flight `injuries.yml` run clobbers `picks.json` with a stale version after `analyst.yml` pushes new picks between the injuries checkout and commit. 4/10 incident: re-run #3 Analyst committed 33 picks for 2026-04-10 at 15:56:44 PT, and 6 seconds later (15:56:50 PT) an injuries.yml run pushed `Lineup update: picks amended` which reverted picks.json to the pre-rerun 15-pick state — two further lineup commits chained on top of the clobbered state before the incident was noticed. Manually recovered via Option-C merge in commit `a131c1f` (see prior entry). This fix ships an automatic version of the same recovery logic as a guard in the commit path. **Implementation:** (1) New standalone script `ingest/merge_picks.py` compares a local (post-lineup_watch or post-lineup_update) picks.json against the origin (post-`git pull --rebase`) version. If origin has MORE today-picks than local, the analyst must have pushed a new pick set during our run — use origin as the base and overlay local's injury-mutation fields onto matching picks (by key `(player_name.lower(), prop_type, pick_value, date)`). Mutation fields carried from local → origin: `voided`, `void_reason`, `lineup_risk`, `injury_status_at_check`, `injury_check_time`, `lineup_update`. Every other field on each pick is trusted from origin. On any uncaught exception the script falls back to copying local → output and exits 1 — preserving current (pre-guard) behavior so the guard can never make things worse than the status quo. Matches the exact recovery logic that was proven to work on the 4/10 incident. (2) `.github/workflows/injuries.yml` commit path modified in two places: (a) the "Commit picks status" step (after `lineup_watch.py`) and (b) the "Commit lineup amendments" step (after `lineup_update.py`). Each step now, after `git pull --rebase origin main`: (i) saves origin's picks.json to `data/picks.json.origin`, (ii) runs `python ingest/merge_picks.py --local --origin --output` to produce the merged picks.json, (iii) cleans up the `.local` and `.origin` temp files, (iv) falls back to direct `mv "$f.local" "$f"` if either file is missing. The "Commit lineup amendments" step additionally skips picks.json in the original `mv "$f.local" "$f"` restore loop so `opportunity_flags.json` is still restored directly (no race concern for that file — it's an accumulating-log file that only lineup_update writes). The first commit step ("Commit injuries") is unchanged because it doesn't touch picks.json. **Unit tests (5 scenarios via synthetic picks):** (a) Normal path — local and origin have the same today-pick count → no-op, local preserved with its mutations ✓; (b) **Race condition** — local has 15 today-picks, origin has 33 (the 4/10 incident pattern) → MERGE TRIGGERED, origin used as base, 3 overlap picks receive local's `voided`/`lineup_update`/`injury_status_at_check` mutations, 30 fresh picks preserved, 12 local-only phantom picks correctly dropped ✓; (c) Error path — local file is corrupt JSON → falls back to copying local verbatim, exits 1, preserves pre-guard behavior ✓; (d) Analyst reduction — local has 20 picks, origin has 15 → guard doesn't fire (20 ≤ 15 is false), local wins, mutations preserved ✓; (e) Empty today-slate — both 0 today-picks → no-op ✓. **Known limitations** (not blocking; flagged for future hardening if needed): (i) Analyst re-runs that *reduce* pick count (e.g. 33 → 20) are NOT caught by the guard because the heuristic is "origin has more" — the smaller set would get clobbered back to the larger local set. This is rare and recoverable via the same manual process used for the 4/10 incident. (ii) Same-count-but-different-picks scenarios are also not caught. Both edge cases are strict improvements over status quo. **Not touched** per spec: `agents/analyst.py`, `agents/lineup_watch.py`, `agents/lineup_update.py`, `agents/auditor.py`, `agents/parlay.py`, `agents/build_site.py`, `agents/quant.py`, `.github/workflows/analyst.yml`, `.github/workflows/auditor.yml`, `.github/workflows/ingest.yml`. `ingest/merge_picks.py` (NEW), `.github/workflows/injuries.yml` (commit steps 2 and 3 only — step 1 "Commit injuries" unchanged). |
| **Parlay: FADE pre-filter + candidate diversification (2026-04-10)** | Moves the "max 1 FADE leg per parlay" constraint from the Claude prompt into Python pre-filtering inside `build_candidates()`, and adds candidate-pool diversification to prevent a single dominant player from monopolizing the top-N candidates sent to Claude. Root-cause incident: on 4/10, `build_candidates()` produced 15 top candidates where **every single one contained Kawhi Leonard** (his high raw confidence inflated composite scores despite FADE edge). Claude tried to reason through the unresolvable constraint tension ("max 1 FADE leg" when all 15 combos had multiple FADE legs) and output prose analysis instead of JSON, which would have crashed the parlay step (now gracefully handled by the empty-result fallback shipped in the prior fix, but the root cause — unresolvable constraint tension — still needed a Python-side solution). Design principle: **constraint satisfaction (filtering) belongs in Python; curation (selecting the best) belongs in the LLM.** **Three-part fix in `agents/parlay.py` only:** (1) **FADE pre-filter** — new block in `build_candidates()` immediately after the existing trim/human-review check counts `recommendation_tier == "FADE"` legs in each combo; combos with 2+ FADE legs are `continue`d. Graceful when `bet_recommendation` is absent (pre-odds-enrichment days) — the `.get()` chain returns `None`, equality check fails, count stays at 0, combo survives the filter. Every candidate Claude now receives has at most 1 FADE leg — the "all combos have 2+ FADE legs" paralysis scenario is impossible by construction. (2) **Candidate diversification** — after the sort-by-composite-score, if any single player appears in more than 80% of the top `TOP_N_TO_CLAUDE` (15) candidates, the bottom third of the top-N is replaced with the best-scored candidates from the remaining pool that exclude the dominant player. Uses `Counter` from `collections` to count player appearances across the top 15; log line prints the dominant player name, their count, and the number of alternatives substituted in (e.g. `[parlay] Diversity fix: Kawhi Leonard appeared in 15/15 top candidates — replaced bottom 5 with alternatives`). When no alternatives exist (genuine monopoly), the top-N is returned unchanged — graceful degradation. Early return if `len(candidates) <= TOP_N_TO_CLAUDE` skips the diversity check entirely for small candidate pools. (3) **Prompt FADE rules softened to advisory** — the hard constraint "Never include 2+ FADE legs in the same parlay" (rule 6) is replaced with "Candidates with 2+ FADE legs have already been filtered out — every candidate below has at most 1 FADE leg. When a candidate has exactly 1 FADE leg, prefer combos where the other legs are POSITIVE or STRONG to compensate." The AVOID item "Parlays where more than one leg has edge_tier='FADE'" is replaced with "Parlays where the single allowed FADE leg is the weakest leg by confidence AND the other legs are all NEUTRAL — prefer combos where at least one non-FADE leg is POSITIVE or STRONG." Both changes move the language from prescriptive constraint to advisory selection guidance. **Unit tests (synthetic data):** (a) 3 FADE + 2 POSITIVE picks → 3 candidates returned, all with ≤1 FADE leg; (b) 5 all-FADE picks → 0 candidates returned (empty list, no crash, graceful degradation — `main()` short-circuits to `sys.exit(0)` via the prior fix); (c) Dominant "Star" player forced into every top candidate → diversity log line fires, bottom 5 replaced with alternatives, final distribution 10 with Star + 5 without (67% Star, down from 100%); (d) Dominant player with incompatible odds → odds-window filter independently prevents monopoly (0/15 contain the dominant player, proving the other filters still work correctly alongside diversification). **Untouched:** `score_combination()` (composite score formula), odds window filter, negative correlation filter, trim filter, `load_todays_picks()`, `load_player_stats()`, `enforce_concentration_cap()`, `call_parlay_agent()` (graceful-failure fix from earlier in this session), `save_parlays()`, `main()` flow. `agents/parlay.py` only. |
| **Parlay: graceful failure + empty-result handling (2026-04-10)** | parlay graceful failure handling — `call_parlay_agent()` now returns `[]` instead of `sys.exit(1)` on parse failure, with `json_repair` fallback, explicit empty-array check, API error catch, and main() short-circuit on zero parlays. Root-cause incident: on 4/10, 30 picks were generated and odds-enriched successfully, but `parlay.py` crashed with `sys.exit(1)` when Claude returned prose analysis (explaining why it couldn't build valid parlays due to too many FADE legs) instead of a JSON array. Parlay runs BEFORE the commit step in `analyst.yml`, so the crash killed the workflow and prevented all 30 picks from being committed to the repo — parlays are supplementary, a parlay failure should never block pick deployment. **Three-part fix in `agents/parlay.py` only:** (1) `call_parlay_agent()` rewritten — the line-583 `sys.exit(1)` on parse failure is replaced with `return []`, and all downstream failure paths also `return []` instead of raising. New `try/except` around the `client.messages.create()` call catches API errors (timeout, rate limit, auth) and returns `[]` with a warning log. New explicit-empty-array check (`if raw.strip() in ("[]", "[ ]")`) catches the clean case where Claude correctly determined no valid parlays exist. New Fallback 1 (bracket-match extraction) tightened to use `rfind("]")` for proper slice bounds. New Fallback 2 (`json_repair` via the already-installed `json_repair` library used by `analyst.py`) attempts one more recovery before giving up. Final failure path logs the raw response preview and returns `[]`. The ONLY remaining `sys.exit(1)` is the missing-API-key config guard at line 551 — every other failure path now degrades gracefully. (2) `build_parlay_prompt()` OUTPUT FORMAT section extended with an explicit empty-array escape hatch: "If no valid parlays can be constructed from the candidates (e.g. too many FADE legs, insufficient POSITIVE/STRONG legs to anchor a parlay, all combos violate the edge quality rules), return an empty JSON array: `[]`" plus a reinforcing line "Returning `[]` is explicitly acceptable and preferred over reasoning about why parlays can't be built. NEVER output prose analysis — always output a JSON array, even if it's empty." This fixes the root cause of the 4/10 incident: Claude's prose response was reasonable behavior because the prompt never told it what to do when no valid parlays existed. (3) `main()` post-Claude block adds a graceful short-circuit — if `call_parlay_agent()` returns `[]`, print "No parlays to save — skipping save step" and `sys.exit(0)`. This bypasses `enforce_concentration_cap()` and `save_parlays()` entirely, avoiding writing an empty bundle to `parlays.json` on days when no valid parlays can be constructed. **Spec invariants verified:** (a) exactly one `sys.exit(1)` remains in the file (the API key config check); (b) the new failure path (Claude returns prose → parse fails → returns `[]` → main() prints skip message → `sys.exit(0)`) allows `analyst.yml` to continue to the commit step and deploy picks; (c) all existing logic untouched — `build_candidates()`, `score_combination()`, `enforce_concentration_cap()`, `save_parlays()`, `load_todays_picks()`, `load_player_stats()` are all unchanged; (d) FADE leg limits, edge quality rules, and parlay selection criteria in the prompt are unchanged (only the output escape hatch was added). `agents/parlay.py` only — no other files touched. Downstream effect: parlay parse failures are now non-fatal, parlay runs on "unfavorable" days (too many FADE legs) cleanly produce zero parlays, and the 4/10 incident class of workflow-killing crashes is eliminated. |
| **Frontend: Display calibrated confidence on pick cards (2026-04-10)** | Pick card headline confidence now shows `bet_recommendation.calibrated_prob` (the system's actual expected hit rate after historical calibration) instead of the raw stated `confidence_pct`. Raw stated confidence moved to the Odds + Sizing drawer as the first line (`System conf: X%`). **Motivation:** the previous display created a visual mismatch — the card showed "84% conf" next to "NEUTRAL (+2.8pp)" but the user couldn't reconcile the numbers because the edge calculation uses the calibrated value (88.3%), not the raw 84%. Now the headline and the edge are visually consistent: e.g., Tyrese Maxey PTS T20 on 4/10 shows `85% conf` with `FADE (-8.5pp)`, which reads as 85 − 93.3 ≈ −8.3 (rounds to the displayed -8.5). **Three-part implementation in `agents/build_site.py` only:** (1) New JS helper `displayConf(p)` returns `Math.round(bet_recommendation.calibrated_prob)` when available, falls back to `confidence_pct` when `bet_recommendation` is null/absent/NO_MARKET. The fallback preserves pre-odds-integration behavior for any pick without market data. (2) Three headline render sites updated: regular pick card (`<div class="conf-line">`), top-picks card (`<div class="tp-conf">`), best-bets card (`<div class="tp-conf">`). All three now use `${displayConf(p)}% conf` instead of `${p.confidence_pct}% conf`. No CSS changes — the existing `conf-line` and `tp-conf` classes use flat colors (`var(--muted)` and `var(--accent)`) so there was no conditional color logic to preserve. (3) `buildOddsSizing()` drawer gained a new first line `System conf: X%` sourced from `p.confidence_pct`, guarded by `!= null` so picks with missing confidence still render cleanly. Placed above Market line as the first drawer item to group system-side info at the top. **Untouched per spec:** `bet_recommendation` computation in `ingest/odds_today.py`, `confidence_pct` on picks (still the raw stated value in the data), `buildEdgeLine()` (still reads `br.recommendation_tier` + `br.calibrated_edge_pct`), Results tab pick history (shows raw `confidence_pct` in the historical table), Parlays tab leg display, lineup-update morning/revised reasoning text, and Python-side scoring logic in `get_top_picks()` + best-bets sort tiebreaker (still uses raw `confidence_pct` for ranking). **Browser-verified** on the 2026-04-10 15-pick slate: 15 regular pick cards and 3 top-picks cards all rendered with calibrated values (85, 88, 85, …); sample drawer showed `System conf: 74%` as the first line; 18 edge badges rendered unchanged with correct FADE/NEUTRAL/STRONG coloring. `agents/build_site.py` only. |
| **Analyst: Scout token budget + shortlist validation fix (2026-04-10)** | Root cause: `SCOUT_MAX_TOKENS = 4096` physically limited the Scout call to ~8-9 structured shortlist entries before JSON truncation, because each entry in the compact Scout output schema requires ~400–500 tokens (player name + team + props + tier ranges + priority + notes). The Scout prompt said "Target 20–25 players" but the output budget made that impossible. On 2026-04-10, a 57-player slate produced a Scout shortlist of only 8 players — the JSON repair path triggered and the Pick stage never saw strong candidates like Brunson (PTS≥20 at 75%), KAT (PTS≥15 at 85%), OG Anunoby (PTS≥10 at 90%), or 40+ others. The model was pre-filtering aggressively to avoid mid-JSON truncation. **Three-part fix in `agents/analyst.py` only:** (1) `SCOUT_MAX_TOKENS` raised 4096 → 12288 (25 entries × 500 tokens + preamble overhead = ~12,500 tokens; 12288 gives headroom without waste). The Scout output is pure JSON with no tier_walk reasoning, so token density is predictable. (2) New "shortlist undersize check" in `main()` immediately after `shortlist_names` is printed: if `active_count >= 40` AND `len(shortlist_names) < 12`, print a warning and fall back to single-call `build_prompt()` mode which sees the entire quant context. Uses the identical fallback pattern as the existing `<5 matched` check (same `build_prompt()` args, same `save_picks`/`save_skips` + `return` sequence). Gated on large slates only — normal-slate Scout behavior (<40 active players) is unchanged. (3) `build_scout_prompt()` INCLUSION GUIDANCE rewritten with stronger imperative language: "CRITICAL: You are the only gate between 57 eligible players and the Pick agent. Any player you exclude here CANNOT receive a pick today — there is no second chance." Explicitly names B2B, tough defense, and blowout risk as NON-reasons to exclude (those are Pick agent penalty rules, not Scout gates). Explicitly forbids the Scout from applying tier-walk or confidence penalty reasoning — that's the Pick agent's job. Cost impact: ~$0.03–0.05 per run at Opus pricing (the large-slate Scout model), negligible vs the ~$0.36/day total. `agents/analyst.py` only — no changes to `call_scout()` JSON parsing, `call_analyst()`, `call_review()`, `build_pick_prompt()`, `build_review_prompt()`, `MAX_TOKENS`, `MODEL`, `MODEL_LARGE`, or `LARGE_SLATE_THRESHOLD`. |
| **Backtest: H26 star absence teammate impact (2026-04-10)** | New `--mode star-absence` added to `agents/backtest.py`. Motivated by 4/9 Tatum scenario — his PTS pick was penalty-skipped but he scored 24 on a T20 when Jaylen Brown was confirmed OUT. Measures teammate tier hit rate deltas (with vs without the team's leading scorer) across PTS/REB/AST/3PM at every valid tier. **Implementation:** new module constants `SA_MIN_STAR_GAMES=20` (games to qualify as team's leading scorer), `SA_MIN_ABSENT_GAMES=5` (minimum star-absent games to analyze a team), `SA_MIN_CONDITION_N=3` (minimum games per with/without bucket per teammate). `STAR_ABSENCE_JSON = DATA / "backtest_star_absence.json"`. New `run_star_absence_analysis(player_log, args)` function: (1) loads the raw `player_game_log.csv` directly so DNP rows are available for absence detection (the shared `load_player_log()` already filters DNPs out); (2) applies `--start` / `--end` / `--season` filters to the full DataFrame; (3) identifies each team's leading scorer from the DNP-filtered `player_log` by highest PTS avg with ≥20 games, broken by `drop_duplicates(subset=team, keep=first)` after sorting PTS avg descending; (4) for each qualifying team, computes star-absent dates as `team_dates − star_played_dates` (team played but star didn't — DNP or missing row entirely); (5) per teammate, splits rows by `_star_absent` flag and computes tier hit rate deltas at every tier; (6) population-level aggregation across all teams uses weighted average by `min(n_with, n_without)` with unweighted comparison and positive-delta percentage; (7) verdict section prints SIGNAL / NOISE / negative classification at key tiers (PTS_T15/T20/T25, AST_T4/T6). Mode wired into `main()` dispatch between `elite-opp-rebounder` and the calibration-only fast path. `--mode` help string extended with `'star-absence'`. **Production run result (14 teams, 31 teammate observations, 2025-10-21 → 2026-04-09):** PTS_T15 +11.3pp (77% positive), PTS_T20 +12.7pp (71% positive), PTS_T25 +10.5pp (71% positive), AST_T4 +9.6pp (71% positive), AST_T6 +6.7pp (55% positive) — all five key tiers cross the +3pp SIGNAL threshold with ≥10 observations. Motivating BOS scenario confirmed: Tatum PTS T20 with Brown=72.7% / without Brown=100% (4 games), Δ=+27.3pp; Pritchard PTS T20 with=28.8% / without=100% (6 games), Δ=+71.2pp. Invariant check: 31/31 teammate `n_with + n_without` matches raw ground truth (no double-counting). **One bug found and fixed during verification:** initial sort key `x.split("T")[1]` crashed on PTS tier keys because `"PTS_T20".split("T") == ['P', 'S_', '20']`; fixed to `x.split("_T")[1]`. Downstream consumers (not yet wired): skip re-evaluation feature in `lineup_update.py` and absence-driven analyst confidence rule; both deferred pending multi-season verification and confirmed-OUT gate alignment with existing Without-Star Baseline rule philosophy. `agents/backtest.py` only — no other files touched. |

The spec's accountability invariant holds: every target player ends up in exactly one of `player_notes` (with items that survived Claude summarization) / `no_id_errors` / `espn_errors` / `no_news_players` / implicit "items fetched but not noteworthy" (raw items present but Claude produced no note). | **Odds: morning baseline capture + pre-tip sweep timing fix (2026-04-10)** | Two related bugs that together prevented `morning_implied_prob` from ever being written to `picks.json`, blocking CLV computation in `auditor.save_audit()`. **Primary fix** — `ingest/odds_today.py main()` now writes `morning_implied_prob` directly in its match block (after `odds_fetched_at`), guarded by `if "morning_implied_prob" not in pick`. Previously only `pretip_sweep()` wrote this field, and pretip was failing to execute due to timing issues (see secondary). Re-run safe: the guard preserves the original baseline across same-day re-runs of `main()`. **Secondary fix** — `pretip_sweep()` timing relaxed to survive GitHub Actions cron delays: new module constant `PRETIP_GRACE_MINUTES = 30` allows capture of games that started up to 30 minutes ago (FanDuel pre-game lines linger briefly after tip); default `window_minutes` widened from 75 → 360 (6h) in both the function signature and the argparse default — combined with existing event_id deduplication, this costs nothing extra (each game is still fetched at most once). Filter updated from `minutes_to_tip < 0` to `minutes_to_tip < -PRETIP_GRACE_MINUTES`. Log lines + docstring updated to reflect new grace window. **Workflow fix** — `.github/workflows/odds_pretip.yml` cron schedule rewritten from 10 entries every 30 min 3:00–7:30 PM PT → 8 entries hourly noon–7 PM PT. GitHub's typical 1–6h cron delays meant the old 3 PM start almost always executed after games had tipped; starting at noon gives 4+ hours of buffer before earliest tip-offs. Design invariant after the fix: every matched pick has both `market_implied_prob` AND `morning_implied_prob` after the morning `analyst.yml` run; if pretip later executes it overwrites `market_implied_prob` with pre-tip odds but leaves `morning_implied_prob` untouched; CLV = `market_implied_prob (pretip) − morning_implied_prob (morning)`. If pretip never runs, the two fields stay equal and CLV degrades gracefully to 0 (no movement detected). Verification: grep confirms `morning_implied_prob` in both `main()` and `pretip_sweep()` under the same guard; `PRETIP_GRACE_MINUTES` referenced in constant, filter, docstring, and log lines; `360` in both function signature and argparse default; 8 cron entries in workflow file; `python ingest/odds_today.py --help` shows all three modes with `--window-minutes` default 360. `ingest/odds_today.py`, `.github/workflows/odds_pretip.yml`. |

| **ESPN Playoff Career Backfill script (2026-04-09)** | New standalone local-run script `ingest/espn_playoff_backfill.py` fetches 2021–2025 regular season AND playoff gamelogs for active whitelisted players from the ESPN public v3 gamelog endpoint (`site.web.api.espn.com/apis/common/v3/sports/basketball/nba/athletes/{id}/gamelog`). Actual ESPN response format differs from all three patterns in the original spec: top-level `labels` list, top-level `events` dict keyed by event_id (game metadata), and `seasonTypes[].categories[].events[]` with inline `{eventId, stats:[array]}` parallel to the top-level labels. Season type filtering via `_season_type_matches()` accepts `Postseason` for type 3 and `Regular Season` (including Play-In Regular Season) for type 2; `Preseason` skipped. API returns all season types regardless of `seasontype` query param — parser filters by `displayName` substring. Legacy Pattern B/C parsers kept as fallbacks. | **Post-processor greedy regex fix — `reconcile_pick_values()` (2026-04-08)** | Strategy 1 regex in `reconcile_pick_values()` used `[^\d]*` (unbounded non-digit gap) between step keywords and destination tier digits. Matched `2` from `B2B` prose ~40 chars after a `→` keyword, producing false AST T4→T2 corrections. Two picks affected on 4/8 (SGA AST, Fox AST) — both overridden to T2, then tagged NO_MARKET (no FanDuel line at AST T2). Fix: `[^\d]*` → `[^\d]{0,20}` caps the gap to 20 characters. Legitimate step-down patterns span ≤12 chars. One-tier-step guard and Strategy 2 regex unchanged. `agents/analyst.py` only — single regex edit in `reconcile_pick_values()`. |
| **Odds calibration key mismatch fix (2026-04-08)** | `_load_calibration_bands()` in `ingest/odds_today.py` read `audit_summary.json["confidence_calibration"]` — correct key is `"confidence_calibration_totals"`. Also: band keys used `"70-75%"` format but actual schema uses `"70-75"` (no `%` suffix); field read `"rate"` but actual schema uses `"hit_rate_pct"` (percentage, not decimal). All three mismatches caused silent fallback to raw stated confidence as calibrated probability, making edge systematically negative and every pick tagged FADE. Fixed: key → `confidence_calibration_totals`, band keys → `"70-75"/"76-80"/"81-85"/"86+"`, field → `hit_rate_pct` with `/100.0` conversion. Verified: stated 80% now maps to cal 87.4% (actual band hit rate). `ingest/odds_today.py` only. |

| **Calibration-Corrected Edge Enrichment — `ingest/odds_today.py` (2026-04-07)** | Added `compute_edge()` function to `ingest/odds_today.py`. Reads confidence calibration bands from `audit_summary.json`, maps each pick's stated confidence to the band's actual historical hit rate (calibrated probability), computes edge vs market implied probability, derives quarter-Kelly fraction, and assigns a recommendation tier (STRONG/POSITIVE/NEUTRAL/FADE/NO_MARKET). Writes `bet_recommendation` sub-object to each today's pick in `picks.json`. Three new functions: `_load_calibration_bands()` (reads `audit_summary.json` confidence_calibration), `_get_calibrated_prob()` (maps stated confidence to calibrated probability via band lookup), `compute_edge()` (orchestrates enrichment for all today's picks). New constant: `AUDIT_SUMMARY_JSON`. `main()` refactored: compute_edge runs after odds annotation, single atomic write for both odds and edge data. Graceful degradation: missing audit_summary or calibration data falls back to stated confidence as probability. Recommendation tier thresholds: STRONG >+8pp, POSITIVE +3–8pp, NEUTRAL ±3pp, FADE <−3pp. Quarter-Kelly formula: `(edge / (odds_decimal - 1)) / 4`, floored at 0. `ingest/odds_today.py` only — no workflow or agent changes. |

| **Empty injury report drawer on frontend after Analyst workflow — `analyst.yml` (2026-04-07)** | Added `data/injuries_today.json` to the `FILES` preservation list in `analyst.yml` commit step. The morning Rotowire refresh (run as the first step of `analyst.yml`) wrote a fresh `injuries_today.json`, but the copy-aside/clean-checkout/rebase/restore pattern in the commit step did not include it — `git checkout -- .` wiped the file before `build_site.py` could read it, producing an empty injury dropdown on the deployed frontend. `.github/workflows/analyst.yml` only — 1 line changed. |
| **Git rebase autostash conflict fix — all workflow files (2026-04-05)** | Replaced `git rebase --autostash origin/main` with a copy-aside/clean-checkout/rebase/restore pattern in all 5 workflow commit steps across `injuries.yml` (3 steps), `analyst.yml`, `auditor.yml`, `ingest.yml`, `odds.yml`. Root cause: `--autostash` stashes local changes before rebase, then `stash pop` conflicts when remote also modified the same data file (e.g. `injuries_today.json`). With injuries running every 30 min, two overlapping runs or a concurrent workflow push would trigger this reliably. New pattern: (1) `cp` freshly-generated files to `.local` copies, (2) `git checkout -- .` to clean working tree, (3) `git pull --rebase origin main` (no stash needed), (4) `mv .local` copies back. Local data is always freshest — correct file always wins. Triggered by 2026-04-05 injuries.yml failure: `U data/injuries_today.json` unmerged conflict after autostash pop. `.github/workflows/injuries.yml`, `.github/workflows/analyst.yml`, `.github/workflows/auditor.yml`, `.github/workflows/ingest.yml`, `.github/workflows/odds.yml`. |

Pipeline crashed on 2026-04-05 large-slate day (31 players) when Claude omitted the `reasoning` field from a pick object. The crash occurred in the summary print loop after picks were already written to `picks.json` — non-destructive but caused process exit code 1, blocking downstream parlay + deploy steps. `agents/analyst.py` only — single line in `save_picks()`. |
| **pick_value output contract — `agents/analyst.py` (2026-04-01)** | Added explicit rule to both `build_pick_prompt()` and `build_prompt()` that emitted `pick_value` must ALWAYS equal the final stepped-down tier threshold, not the pre-step original tier. Contract placed adjacent to `pick_value` field definition in output format section; reinforcing reminder added to TIER_WALK FORMAT section. Audit evidence: Harden AST T6→T4 step-down 2026-03-31 — tier_walk correctly stated "b2b <5g → step down → T4" but `pick_value=6` was emitted instead of 4. `agents/analyst.py` only — prompt text in both functions. |
| **Minimum-tier REB confidence cap — `agents/analyst.py` (2026-04-01)** | New prompt rule in both `build_pick_prompt()` and `build_prompt()`: when a REB pick is at T4 (minimum valid REB tier) AND `b2b_hit_rates` is null for REB (`b2b <5g`), cap final confidence at 72% regardless of overall hit rate, iron_floor status, or trend direction. Tier_walk must flag explicitly: "minimum-tier REB, no B2B validation — confidence capped at 72%." Rationale: T4 is the floor — the system cannot step lower; when B2B sample is also absent, the combined uncertainty cannot be fully absorbed by -5% adjustment alone. Stacks with existing B2B <5g one-tier-down penalty. Audit evidence: Harden REB T4 2026-03-31 — 0 actual in 28 min, 78% confidence, competitive road game. `agents/analyst.py` only — prompt text in both functions. |
| **VOLATILE + iron_floor 3PM incompatibility — `agents/analyst.py` (2026-04-01)** | New prompt rule in both `build_pick_prompt()` and `build_prompt()`: when a 3PM prop has BOTH `iron_floor=true` AND the VOLATILE tag, iron_floor is treated as OVERRIDDEN for that prop. Standard non-iron-floor 3PM rules apply; confidence capped at 80% regardless of B2B hit rate, historical floor rate, or trend. iron_floor must not be cited as supporting factor in tier_walk. Rationale: iron_floor is valid for creation-based props (AST, low-threshold REB) where output floor is role-structural; for 3PM, the floor depends on shot attempts and a VOLATILE shooter can produce 0 makes on 0 attempts. Audit evidence: Donovan Mitchell 3PM T2 2026-03-31 — iron_floor=true + VOLATILE, 0 actual in 24 min, 91% B2B iron_floor pick. `agents/analyst.py` only — prompt text in both functions. |
| **Amendment gates: sub-70% auto-skip + B2B <5g upside block — `agents/lineup_update.py` (2026-04-01)** | Two deterministic gates added to `apply_amendments()`. **Gate 1 (Sub-70% auto-skip):** when `direction=="down"` and `revised_confidence_pct < 70`, the pick is immediately voided. The `lineup_update` sub-object remains on the voided pick for audit trail. Fixes SGA AST T4 miss 2026-03-30 (amended to 68%, ran anyway). **Gate 2 (B2B <5g upside block):** when `direction=="up"` and `player_stats[player].b2b_hit_rates[prop]` is null (fewer than 5 B2B games) AND player is `on_back_to_back`, the amendment is overridden to `direction="unchanged"` with original confidence preserved. Opponent lineup changes do not resolve B2B sample uncertainty. Fixes Harden AST T4 + REB T6 misses 2026-03-31 (both had null B2B hit rates, both amended up, both missed). Function signature extended with `player_stats: dict \| None = None`; call site passes `player_stats=player_stats`. `agents/lineup_update.py` only — 3 edits. |

| **Amendment sub-70% auto-skip — `agents/lineup_update.py` (2026-03-31)** | Added deterministic gate in `apply_amendments()`. When a lineup amendment revises confidence below 70% with `direction="down"`, the pick is immediately voided with `void_reason` referencing the revised confidence. The `lineup_update` sub-object and its reasoning remain visible on the voided pick. Fixes 2026-03-30 SGA AST T4 miss (amended to 68%, ran anyway). `agents/lineup_update.py` only. |
| **Overload retry logic — `agents/analyst.py` (2026-03-31)** | Added `_call_with_overload_retry` helper and retry loops in `call_scout()` and `call_analyst()`. Exponential backoff: 10s/20s/40s/80s, 4 retries. Scout retries before falling back to single-call mode; analyst retries before raising. Fixes 2026-03-31 complete run failure due to unhandled `overloaded_error`. `agents/analyst.py` only. |
| **Diagnostic files committed for git history (2026-03-26)** | Added `pre_game_news.json` and `team_defense_narratives.json` to `analyst.yml` commit loop; added `post_game_news.json` to `auditor.yml` commit loop. All three files were already written and consumed correctly within their workflows — this change preserves them in git for retroactive debugging of miss classifications and pre-game context. `scout_omitted_*.json` glob was already removed from analyst.yml in the earlier Scout omitted cleanup. `.github/workflows/analyst.yml`, `.github/workflows/auditor.yml` — 1 line changed each. |
| **Without [X] context line gated on teammate OUT status (2026-03-26)** | `build_quant_context()` now only renders the `Without [teammate]` line when the named teammate is confirmed OUT/OFS in `injuries_today.json`. Previously rendered whenever `key_teammate_absent` had ≥3 historical absence games, even when the teammate was healthy and playing today — showing misleading baseline data as if it were active context. Added `players_out_today: set[str] | None = None` parameter to `build_quant_context()` and `load_players_out_today()` helper (returns full player names with OUT/OFS status). Gate condition: `kta.get("teammate_name", "") in _out_set`. Both call sites in `main()` pass `_players_out_names`. Matches the trend override gate added to `build_player_stats()` on 2026-03-25. `agents/analyst.py` only. |
| **standings_today.json committed by ingest.yml (2026-03-26)** | `data/standings_today.json` was written by `espn_daily_ingest.py` in `ingest.yml` but never committed there. `auditor.yml` chains directly off `ingest.yml` and reads the file for the `## PLAYOFF PICTURE` block — but got a fresh checkout with stale/missing standings. Added to ingest.yml FILES array. `.github/workflows/ingest.yml` only — 1 line added. |
| **parlays.json committed by auditor.yml (2026-03-26)** | `data/parlays.json` grading results (`result`, `legs_hit`, `leg_results`) were written by `auditor.py` but never committed by `auditor.yml` — parlay grading results were silently discarded after every auditor run since launch. The frontend Parlays tab was showing ungraded parlays indefinitely. Added to auditor.yml commit step `for` loop. `.github/workflows/auditor.yml` only — 1 line changed. |
| **lineups_today.json committed by injuries.yml (2026-03-26)** | `data/lineups_today.json` was written to the runner disk by `rotowire_injuries_only.py` during hourly injury refreshes but never committed — the file disappeared when the runner exited. Added to the `injuries.yml` commit step `for` loop alongside `injuries_today.json` and `injury_log.csv`. This ensures lineup data (starters + projected minutes) persists across hourly runs and is available to `lineup_update.py` and `analyst.py` in subsequent workflow checkouts. `.github/workflows/injuries.yml` only — 1 line changed. |
| **Projected minutes integer extraction fix (2026-03-26)** | Fixed `parse_projected_minutes()` returning 0 minutes for every player despite finding them correctly. `el.parent` was the `<a>` tag's immediate wrapper (containing only the player name); the minutes integer is a sibling text node inside the enclosing `<li>`. Changed to `el.find_parent("li") or el.parent` so `get_text()` captures the full list item including the integer. `ingest/rotowire_injuries_only.py` only — 1 line changed. |
| **Road underdog near-threshold PTS penalty (2026-03-26)** | Added `ROAD UNDERDOG NEAR-THRESHOLD PTS PENALTY` to KEY RULES — SPREAD / BLOWOUT RISK in both `build_prompt()` and `build_pick_prompt()`. -5% confidence when: away team, spread_abs 4–7 (positive spread = underdog), raw_avgs PTS − pick_value ≤ 5 (near-threshold cushion). Iron_floor exempts. Addresses underdog-side blowout risk not covered by existing BLOWOUT_RISK rules (which only fire at spread_abs ≥ 8 for the favored side). Audit evidence: Barnes PTS T10 (raw_avg ~14, cushion=4) missed at 9 when TOR lost by 25 as 4.5-point road underdog at LAC. `agents/analyst.py` only — prompt text in both functions. |
| **volatile_weak_combo PTS skip narrowed (2026-03-26)** | Trigger conditions changed from `(7/10 OR 8/10) + T15+` to `(7/10 only) + T20+`. Audit evidence: 3/3 false skip rate — KD T20 (actual 30), Sengun T15 (actual 30), plus one Ingram instance. 8/10 at any tier is not a weak combination after the mandatory -5% VOLATILE deduction (80% - 5% = 75%, a legitimate pick). T15–T19 VOLATILE picks with 8/10 hit rates now proceed under standard VOLATILE treatment (-5% confidence deduction, no hard skip). Exception (a) baseline text updated from "8/10" to "7/10". Both `build_prompt()` and `build_pick_prompt()` updated identically. `agents/analyst.py` only — prompt text in both functions. |
| **Scout omitted block removed (2026-03-25)** | Removed the Scout omitted block entirely — prompt section, `call_scout()` omitted extraction + sentinel injection, `save_scout_omitted()` function, `SCOUT_OMITTED_JSON` constant, and `analyst.yml` commit glob. The omitted block never populated correctly in 6 consecutive days of production runs (always `[]` or sentinel-injected). Nothing downstream consumed the `scout_omitted_YYYY-MM-DD.json` file. The Review agent (Stage 3) now handles pick coverage concerns. `call_scout()` return type simplified from `tuple[list[dict] | None, list[dict]]` to `list[dict] | None`. All `return None, []` failure paths changed to `return None`. Saves prompt output tokens on every Scout call. `agents/analyst.py`, `.github/workflows/analyst.yml`. |
| **Absence-aware trend activation guard (2026-03-25)** | Fixed bug where absence-aware trend override fired unconditionally — even when the key teammate was healthy and playing today. The override in `build_player_stats()` now requires the key teammate to be confirmed OUT or OFS in `injuries_today.json` before overriding the standard L5-vs-L20 trend. Added `load_players_out_today()` helper (reads injuries file, returns set of OUT/OFS player names) and `players_out_today: set[str] | None = None` parameter to `build_player_stats()`. Gate condition: `_teammate_name in _out_set`. Safe fallback: empty `players_out_today` means override never fires (standard trend always used). The full `key_teammate_absent` dict (including `absence_trend`) is still written to `player_stats.json` regardless — only the trend label override is gated. Root cause: Luka's 3PM trend reflected "without Reaves" stats even though Reaves was healthy, because Reaves had missed some games earlier in the season and `absence_trend` was populated. `agents/quant.py` only — 4 locations changed. |
| **Rotowire parser rewrite (2026-03-25)** | Rewrote three broken parse functions in `ingest/rotowire_injuries_only.py`. (1) `parse_rotowire_lineups` — was returning 0 teams every run; old parser walked ancestor DOM trees looking for `data-team` on container divs, which doesn't exist there. Rewritten to anchor on `data-team` attribute in the On/Off Court Stats `<button>` (same anchor used by the working `parse_rotowire_injuries`); slices HTML between consecutive buttons to isolate each team's Expected Lineup section; reads player names from `<a title="">` attribute (full name) rather than link text (may be abbreviated); detects inline injury status keywords. (2) `parse_projected_minutes` — was returning 0 teams; the `div.lineups-viz` class it searched for does not exist on `projected-minutes.php`. Rewritten to anchor on team logo `<img src="/100{ABBREV}.png">` pattern; walks up ancestors to find player link containers; handles Subscriber Exclusive gating with `break`; extracts STARTERS/BENCH/MAY NOT PLAY/OUT section headers from NavigableString text nodes. (3) `parse_onoff_usage` — On/Off Court Stats panel is JavaScript-loaded via AJAX button click, never present in server-rendered HTML. Replaced 120-line parser with clean `return {}` + diagnostic log. Root cause across all three: page structure had changed; old class-name selectors and ancestor DOM walk patterns were stale. `parse_rotowire_injuries` unchanged (already working). `ingest/rotowire_injuries_only.py` only. |
| **Absence-aware trend fix (2026-03-25)** | `trend` label now overrides standard L5-vs-L20 computation with absence-window-scoped trend when `key_teammate_absent` is active (≥5 absence games). Fixes regime-crossing artifact: players with elevated role post-star-injury showed `trend=up` because L20 baseline included pre-absence lower-usage games. Confirmed: Randle `trend=up→stable` on 2026-03-25 (L5=22.6 vs absence-window=24.6, delta=−8.1%). `absence_trend` dict also stored in `key_teammate_absent` for audit purposes. `agents/quant.py` only — `compute_teammate_absence_splits()` and `build_player_stats()`. |
| **Streak pill removed from pick cards (2026-03-25)** | Pick card streak pills were displaying system-wide prop-type streak (e.g. "system's last 8 PTS picks all hit") rather than player-specific streak, making them actively misleading on individual cards. Removed `streakSpan` variable and `buildMicroStats()` param from pick card rendering loop. Results tab streak cards unchanged. `agents/build_site.py` only — 3 lines changed. |
| **is_skip boolean field — robust skip gate (2026-03-25)** | Added `is_skip: true/false` to pick JSON schema in both `build_pick_prompt()` and `build_prompt()`. `filter_self_skip_picks()` now checks `is_skip=true` as primary gate before regex fallback. Review Step 0 backstop updated to check `is_skip` field first. `save_picks()` defaults `is_skip=false` for picks missing the field. Eliminates regex whack-a-mole for skip detection — boolean field is authoritative, regex patterns remain as fallback. Root cause of recurring skip leaks: every new skip pathway produced new vocabulary no regex covered. `agents/analyst.py` only — 7 locations. |
| **Scout omitted block fix (2026-03-25)** | `scout_omitted_YYYY-MM-DD.json` was returning `[]` for all 6 days since Scout→Pick→Review launch. Two root causes: (1) prompt never told Scout to account for every quant stats player — only that the array must not be empty, which the model ignored; (2) `call_scout()` accepted empty array silently. Fix: rewrote `OMITTED BLOCK` instruction to explicitly require one entry per non-shortlisted player; updated omitted schema comment to reinforce the per-player requirement; added sentinel injection in `call_scout()` as enforcement backstop with `WARNING` log on compliance failure. `agents/analyst.py` only — prompt text + ~10 lines in `call_scout()`. |
| **Team abbreviation mismatch fix (2026-03-25)** | 10 whitelisted players were completely invisible to quant and analyst due to ESPN abbreviation mismatch: `nba_master.csv` and `player_game_log.csv` use ESPN short abbrevs (SA, GS, NY, UTAH) while `player_whitelist.csv` `team_abbr` uses standard NBA abbrevs (SAS, GSW, NYK, UTA). `team_abbr_alt` column already existed in whitelist with correct ESPN values but was never read. Fix: `load_whitelist()` in both `quant.py` and `analyst.py` now emits tuples for both `team_abbr` AND `team_abbr_alt`. Secondary fix: `load_injuries()` in `analyst.py` now normalizes `teams_today` through `_ABBR_NORM` before matching against `injuries_today.json` standard-abbrev keys. | **H19 Finding 2: 3PM blowout trend-down hard skip retired for spread_abs 8–18 (2026-03-22)** | H19 backtest (n=96–137) showed `blowout_win` 3PM hits at 78.8–79.2% (lift=1.097–1.103) — above the 71.8% baseline. Hard skip was blocking above-baseline picks. Players with 24+ minutes in blowout wins get catch-and-shoot opportunities; garbage-time collapse affects sub-24-minute players already excluded from picks. Skip validation also showed 100% false skip rate for `3pm_blowout_trend_down` on Mar 20. | **H19 Finding 1: Secondary Scorer PTS Skip narrowed to spread_abs ≥ 15 (2026-03-22)** | H19 backtest (n=140) showed `blowout_win_secondary` PTS hits at 80.7% (lift=1.083) — above baseline 74.5%. Rule was blocking above-baseline picks at spread_abs 8–14. At spread_abs ≥ 15 blowout is near-certain; skip remains appropriate. | **Blowout secondary scorer skip direction fix (2026-03-20)** | Rule body said "player's team is the large underdog (spread of +8 or worse)" — inverted from the correct trigger. BLOWOUT_RISK=True in quant means the player's team IS the heavily favored side, not the underdog. Confirmed cause: Jalen Green PTS skip on 2026-03-19 (PHX +9.5 underdog) — rule fired on the wrong side. | **Review Agent — Adversarial Pick Stress-Test (2026-03-20)** | Added Review as Stage 3 of the analyst pipeline in `agents/analyst.py`. Review receives per-pick vulnerability cards (volatility, B2B hit rates, blowout risk, minutes floor, bounce_back, FT safety margin) + audit miss pattern summary. Outputs clean/concern/stay_away verdicts per pick. Writes `data/picks_review_YYYY-MM-DD.json` in existing schema (auditor already reads it). Existing manual review files take priority — `apply_review_flags()` skips write if file exists. Failure is non-fatal — picks delivered regardless. Four new functions: `build_review_context()`, `build_review_prompt()`, `call_review()`, `apply_review_flags()`. `build_site.py` updated to show auto-review badges (`🤖 Auto-Review` / `🤖 Stay Away`) distinct from manual review badges (`⚠ Caution` / `⚠ Flagged`). `analyst.yml` updated to commit `picks_review_*.json` files. Review model: always Sonnet; max_tokens: 4096. `agents/analyst.py`, `agents/build_site.py`, `.github/workflows/analyst.yml`. |
| **Scout → Pick two-stage analyst pipeline (2026-03-20)** | Replaced single-call analyst with a two-stage LLM pipeline to fix attention dilution on large slates. **Stage 1 (Scout):** receives all contextual data (quant stats, game logs, season context, news, lineups, profiles, leaderboard, team defense, playoff picture) but NO rules; produces a structured shortlist of 20–25 players with per-player prop-type assessments. Scout model = Opus on large slates (>30 players), Sonnet otherwise. `SCOUT_MAX_TOKENS = 4096`. **Stage 2 (Pick):** receives Scout shortlist + filtered quant stats (shortlisted players only) + full rulebook + audit feedback; no redundant context blocks. Pick model = always Sonnet (shortlist ~20 players, never triggers Opus threshold). **Fallback:** if Scout parse fails or <5 players match quant stats, falls back to original single-call `build_prompt()` + `call_analyst()` path — all legacy functions preserved byte-for-byte. New functions: `build_scout_prompt()`, `call_scout()` (returns None on any failure — never sys.exit), `build_pick_prompt()` (full rulebook from `build_prompt()`, references SCOUT SHORTLIST). `main()` refactored: Scout → shortlist filtering → Pick → `save_picks()`/`save_skips()`. Output schemas (`picks.json`, `skipped_picks.json`) unchanged. `agents/analyst.py` only. |
| **filter_self_skip_picks — hard gate and named skip pattern coverage (2026-03-19)** | Added 7 regex patterns to `SKIP_CONCLUSIONS` in `filter_self_skip_picks()` in `agents/analyst.py`: `HARD GATE FIRES`, `BLOWOUT_SECONDARY_SCORER SKIP fires`, case-insensitive `hard gate fires`, named rule skip phrases (volatile_weak_combo, ast_hard_gate, blowout_secondary_scorer, 3pm_blowout_trend_down, reb_floor_skip, blowout_t25_skip, fg_margin_thin_tier_step), `SKIP T{N} AST/PTS/REB/3PM` + hard gate, `mandatory skip`, `Record as skip`. Previously these tier_walk conclusions were not matched, allowing hard-gate-skipped picks to pass through to `picks.json`. Caught via Banchero AST (ast_hard_gate) and Jalen Green PTS (blowout_secondary_scorer) on 2026-03-19. `agents/analyst.py` only — `filter_self_skip_picks()` SKIP_CONCLUSIONS list. |
| **T25 PTS blowout hard skip (spread_abs ≥ 15) + 3PM confidence floor 75% (2026-03-19)** | Two rule additions to `build_prompt()` in `agents/analyst.py`. **(1) T25 blowout hard skip:** Upgraded spread_abs ≥ 15 T25/T30 PTS from confidence cap (74%) to hard skip (`blowout_t25_skip`). Applies to favored-side only (negative spread). Confirmed by three instances: Jokic Mar 17 (spread 15.5, 8 PTS actual), SGA Mar 18 (spread 19.5, 20 PTS, human manual_skip pre-game), plus ongoing pattern. `PTS T25 BLOWOUT HARD SKIP` rule added to TIER CEILING RULES block; cross-reference note added to ELITE SCORER BLOWOUT EXEMPTION exception clause. `blowout_t25_skip` added to skip_reason enum. **(2) 3PM confidence floor 75%:** Added prop-specific confidence floor of 75% for 3PM picks (system floor is 70%). `3PM CONFIDENCE FLOOR` rule added to SELECTION RULES block. Motivated by binary outcome risk and thin R/R at marginal confidence levels — preserves iron_floor picks at 78%+ while eliminating borderline 71–74% 3PM picks. No skip record needed when floor gates (pick simply does not emit). `agents/analyst.py` only. |
| **fg_margin_thin redesign — step-down cascade not hard skip (2026-03-19)** | Replaced hard skip behavior with full tier step-down cascade (T20→T15→T10→skip). Only skips PTS prop if T10 also fails after full cascade. Renamed skip label from `fg_margin_thin_no_valid_tier` → `fg_margin_thin_tier_step`. Motivated by 100% false skip rate on graded instances (Brown T20 skip → actual 32, Adebayo flagged today). `agents/analyst.py` only — two locations: FG% Safety Margin rule block and skip_reason enum. |
| **Analyst Prompt Rules — Blowout Exemption Cap + VOLATILE AST Gate + Iron-Floor B2B Gate + 3PM Top-Pick Gate (2026-03-18)** | Four prompt-only rules added to `build_prompt()` in `agents/analyst.py`, all motivated by confirmed misses from March 17, 2026 audit. **(1) Elite scorer blowout exemption upper bound:** Jokic PTS T15 miss in a 28-point DEN blowout (spread_abs=15.5, 25 minutes played) showed the existing raw_avgs PTS ≥ 27.0 exemption is too broad at extreme spreads. Fix: added "Exception to the exemption" clause immediately after the existing exemption statement — when spread_abs >= 15, the full 74% blowout confidence cap applies to ALL players regardless of elite scorer status. Exemption still applies in the 8–14 spread range. 27.0 PPG threshold unchanged. **(2) VOLATILE + AST T6 hard block in AST rules section:** Doncic AST T6 miss (actual 4, trim-flagged correctly pre-game) showed the elite playmaker exemption does not protect against floor instability. Added VOLATILE + HIGH AST TIER BLOCK after the AST T4+ HARD GATE section: VOLATILE + AST tier >= T6 = hard SKIP, no exceptions, regardless of elite playmaker exemption status. **(3) Iron-floor B2B road gate for non-primary BHs:** Bane AST T2 miss — B2B road game at OKC (tough defense), 9/10 hit rate, iron_floor tag, actual 1. Fix: IRON-FLOOR B2B ROAD GATE added to REST & FATIGUE block — when on_back_to_back=True AND home_away="A" AND opp_defense=tough AND raw_avgs AST < 6.0, the iron_floor tag does NOT waive the gate; requires opp_defense="soft" to pick AST, otherwise SKIP. **(4) 3PM top-pick requires iron_floor:** Reaves 3PM T1 miss (top_pick=true, 9/10 hit rate, actual 0) and 81–85% 3PM band miscalibration. Fix: 3PM TOP-PICK RESTRICTION added to TOP PICKS block — top_pick=true on 3PM requires iron_floor=true; without iron_floor, cap 3PM confidence at 80% and exclude from top_pick. `agents/analyst.py` only. |
| **Post-Game Reporter + Auditor — in-game injury exit detection fix (2026-03-18)** | Root cause: two confirmed misclassification failures — Cade Cunningham (back spasms, Q1 exit, 5 min) and LaMelo Ball (foul trouble, low minutes) — both returned `event_type="minutes_restriction"` from `post_game_reporter.py` because their exit phrasing ("back spasms", "ruled out for the remainder") was not in `_INJURY_EXIT_TERMS`. Auditor received no injury_exit signal, classified misses as `model_gap_rule`, and generated rule-change recommendations built on a false blowout-management premise. Two-part fix: **(1) `agents/post_game_reporter.py`** — `_INJURY_EXIT_TERMS` extended with 8 new terms ("spasms", "spasm", "ruled out for the remainder", "ruled out for remainder", "did not finish", "did not complete", "hard fall", "took a fall", "fell hard", "carted off", "stretchered", "could not return", "unable to return"); new promotion block added after the existing `no_data` promotion: when `event_type=="minutes_restriction"` AND `from_news=False` (box score inference path) AND `inj_detected=True` AND `minutes < MINUTES_LOW_THRESHOLD`, promote to `injury_exit` with an "inferred" confidence label and log `[post_game_reporter] ↑ name: promoted minutes_restriction → injury_exit`. **(2) `agents/auditor.py`** — STEP 2 in `build_audit_prompt()` now opens with a FAST PATH block: if `event_type=injury_exit` appears in `## POST-GAME NEWS CONTEXT` for a player, classify as `injury_event` immediately without game-script analysis; fast path also checks for `post_game_event="injury_exit"` on the pick object itself. `injury_event` criteria widened: very low minutes (< 10) alone is sufficient regardless of individual stat values (a player can score 6 PTS in 5 minutes and still be an injury exit). New Python annotation pass in `build_audit_prompt()` after `hits_and_misses` is built: iterates `post_game_news`, stamps `post_game_event="injury_exit"` and `post_game_detail` directly onto pick dicts for players with injury_exit events — belt-and-suspenders with the news block. `agents/post_game_reporter.py`, `agents/auditor.py`. |
| **Analyst prompt hardening — three rule additions (2026-03-17)** | Three new directive rules added to `build_prompt()` in `agents/analyst.py`, all motivated by March 15–16 audit evidence. (1) **VOLATILE + AST T6 hard skip (`volatile_ast_t6`):** If a stat is tagged [VOLATILE] AND the selected AST tier is T6 or higher, skip the AST pick entirely — no lower-tier fallback. Elite playmaker exemption (raw_avgs AST ≥ 8.0) does NOT override this rule; that exemption only protects against the low-volume position gate in the AST T4+ HARD GATE. Iron_floor exception: iron_floor AND trend=up at exactly T6 exempts the pick; T8+ skips regardless. Inserted in KEY RULES — VOLATILITY block after the VOLATILE PTS skip exception paragraph. `volatile_ast_t6` added to named skip list in HARD SKIPS priority framework. Audit evidence: Luka Doncic AST T6, actual 4, L10 range 4–13. (2) **3PM confidence ceiling at 80% for non-iron-floor picks:** Do not assign confidence_pct > 80 on any 3PM pick unless iron_floor=true. Cap applied after all other penalties. top_pick=true ineligible on non-iron-floor 3PM picks. Inserted at end of KEY RULES — SEQUENTIAL GAME CONTEXT block, before KEY RULES — INJURY STATUS ON SHOOTING PROPS. Audit evidence: Austin Reaves 3PM T1 at 84% (top_pick=true), 9/10 hit rate, actual 0. (3) **VOLATILE tag neutralizes absence-driven upside arguments:** When [VOLATILE] appears on a stat, do not raise confidence citing teammate/opponent absence — treat as direction unchanged. Genuine role-change reassignments evaluated separately with explicit floor-change reasoning. Iron_floor overrides. Inserted in KEY RULES — VOLATILITY block after the VOLATILE AST skip. Audit evidence: Kevin Durant PTS (VOLATILE) amended 74%→79% citing Sengun OUT — scored 18 on T20 threshold. All three are prompt-only. `agents/analyst.py` only. |
| **JSON repair layer in analyst.py parse_claude_response() (2026-03-17)** | Root cause: analyst run hard-failed on 2026-03-17 when Claude produced structurally valid JSON containing a bad character inside a `tier_walk` string field (`Expecting ',' delimiter at char 81930`). Fix: `_repair_json(raw)` helper added immediately before `call_analyst()` in `agents/analyst.py`. Two-step repair: (1) `json_repair` library attempt (handles unescaped chars, trailing commas, truncated strings); (2) targeted character sanitization — char-by-char scan tracking string state, replaces literal `\n`/`\r`/`\t` inside string values with escaped equivalents. Both except blocks in `call_analyst()` (object-format path and flat-array fallback path) now call `_repair_json()` before `sys.exit(1)`. Repair logs a WARNING (not ERROR) on success so the pick run continues with visible log line. Happy path (valid JSON) is completely unchanged — `_repair_json()` is never called when `json.loads(raw)` succeeds. `json-repair` added to pip install step in `.github/workflows/analyst.yml`. `agents/analyst.py`, `.github/workflows/analyst.yml`. |
| **Picks Review integration — human_verdict field + audit precision + parlay stub + frontend badge (2026-03-16)** | Wires manually-produced daily `data/picks_review_YYYY-MM-DD.json` files into three agents. Review file schema: `[{date, player_name, team, prop_type, pick_value, verdict, trim_reasons}]`; verdicts: "keep"/"trim"/"manual_skip"; join key: `(player_name_lower, prop_type, pick_value)`. (1) `auditor.py`: `PICKS_REVIEW_DIR = DATA` constant; `load_picks_review(date_str)` loads the file and returns `{(name_lower, prop_type, pick_value): entry}` dict; `apply_human_verdicts(graded_picks, review)` tags each graded pick with `human_verdict` and `trim_reasons` (null/[] when not reviewed); both called in `main()` after `grade_picks()`; `save_audit_summary()` extended with `human_flag_precision` block — reads all picks from `picks.json`, groups by `human_verdict`, computes `{hits, misses, total, hit_rate_pct}` per verdict type over full season history. (2) `parlay.py` stub: `PICKS_REVIEW_DIR = DATA` constant; `load_todays_picks_review()` returns `{(name_lower, prop_type, pick_value): verdict}`; `load_todays_picks()` loads review, excludes `manual_skip` picks with log, and carries `_human_verdict` tag on remaining picks; `build_candidates()` enforces max-1-trim-per-card and requires ≥2 clean anchors (non-trim legs) before a trim pick can appear. (3) `build_site.py`: `.review-badge-trim` (amber) and `.review-badge-skip` (red) CSS classes; `reviewVerdict`/`reviewBadge`/`reviewReasons`/`reviewHtml` vars in pick card renderer; `{{reviewHtml}}` injected below `{{statusBadge}}` in card template — renders "⚠ Caution" (trim) or "⚠ Flagged" (manual_skip) with inline reasons; no badge on keep/null. All consumers degrade gracefully when review file absent. `agents/auditor.py`, `agents/parlay.py`, `agents/build_site.py`. |

| **Analyst prompt — meta-framework for rule conflict resolution (2026-03-16)** | Added `KEY FRAMEWORK — HOW TO REASON WHEN RULES CONFLICT` block to `build_prompt()` in `agents/analyst.py`, inserted immediately before `KEY RULES — MATCHUP QUALITY`. Seven components: (1) 5-level priority order for conflicting rules (hard skips → mandatory tier steps → confidence penalties → caps → positive signals); (2) PENALTY STACK LIMIT — >3 independent penalties triggers re-examination or skip; (3) TIER_WALK FORMAT — clean chain documentation requirements; (4) SANITY CHECK — 4-point self-validation gate before emitting each pick, including smell test for incoherent low-tier picks on elite scorers; (5) ON COMPLEX SLATES — frames multi-signal days as normal and manageable; (6) PLAYER TIER CONTEXT — anchors elite scorer recognition to leaderboard block; (7) CONFIDENCE THRESHOLD IS A FLOOR, NOT A TARGET — prevents rounding up from honest sub-70% assessment. Also updated `## SELECTION RULES` confidence threshold line to reinforce floor vs. target distinction. Prompt-only, no Python changes. Motivated by 2026-03-15 SGA T10 cascade failure and recurring workflow_gap misses. `agents/analyst.py` only. |

L20 rank shown with arrow (↑/↓/→, threshold ±3 spots) to flag surging/declining players. | **Knowledge staleness awareness block in analyst build_prompt() (March 10, 2026)** | `## IMPORTANT: YOUR TRAINING KNOWLEDGE IS POTENTIALLY YEARS OUT OF DATE` block inserted in `build_prompt()` between `Today is {TODAY_STR}.` and `## YOUR TASK`. Distinguishes perishable knowledge (player roles and usage, rosters and depth charts, team systems and pace, H2H matchup history, season narratives — do NOT rely on training data for any of these) from durable knowledge (general basketball principles, tier logic and statistical reasoning, role archetype reasoning — apply freely). | **Analyst — three prompt rule hardenings (March 11, 2026)** | (1) **min_floor mandatory tier step-down:** `min_floor < 24 AND tier ≥ T15 → mandatory step to T10` (was: confidence cap only). | **Auditor — Game Results Context Injection (March 12, 2026)** | Root cause addressed: auditor had no direct access to final game scores, forcing it to infer blowout context from ESPN news and Brave Search hits — both unreliable (Durant vs. Jokic HOU/DEN same-game miss asymmetry, March 11, 2026). | **Auditor — voided pick grading bug fix + historical data repair (March 14, 2026)** | Root cause: `grade_picks()` in `auditor.py` had no guard checking `voided` before assigning results. Bug A: picks with `voided=True` (set by `lineup_watch.py`) were falling through the grading loop and receiving `result="MISS"` when the player's box score showed 0 stats (DNP). Bug B: picks with `void_reason` set post-hoc (late-DNP detected) but `voided` not flipped were graded `result="MISS", actual_value=0.0` instead of being promoted to voided. Affected: 4 Derrick White picks (2026-03-12, Bug A) + 2 Alperen Sengun picks (2026-03-13, Bug B). Fix 1A: voided guard added immediately after `p = pick.copy()` in the main grading loop — sets `result=None, actual_value=None` and continues. Fix 1B: second-pass loop added after the main loop (before `return graded`) — detects `result=="MISS" AND actual_value==0.0 AND void_reason set AND not voided`, promotes to `voided=True, result=None`. `build_audit_prompt()` and `save_audit_summary()` were already correct (already split voided/active; denominator already `hits/(hits+misses)`). `scripts/repair_void_grading.py` created — patches Bug A and Bug B in `picks.json`, recomputes affected `audit_log.json` entries (2026-03-12: 84.6%→91.7%, 2026-03-13: 84.0%→91.3%), regenerates `audit_summary.json`. Corrected season: 299H/51M = 85.4% (was 84.0% with 6 corrupted misses inflating denominator). `agents/auditor.py` only for the production fix; `scripts/repair_void_grading.py` is a standalone one-time repair. |
| **Whitelisted teammates grounding (March 14, 2026)** | Fixes stale training data hallucination where the Analyst free-associated historical teammate relationships (e.g. Harden + VanVleet) with no current-season grounding. Three-part fix: (1) `quant.py` `build_player_stats()` — added `whitelisted_teammates: sorted(teammate_corr.keys())` as second field in `stats_out[player_name]` dict, immediately after `"team"`; value is the list of other active whitelisted players on the same team playing today, derived from the already-computed `teammate_corr` dict (zero new computation). (2) `analyst.py` `build_quant_context()` — added `teammates_line` ("  Teammates (active/whitelisted): Name1, Name2") rendered after `momentum_line` in the `lines.append()` block; empty string (not rendered) when no whitelisted teammates playing today. (3) `analyst.py` `build_prompt()` — added `TEAMMATE REFERENCES` guardrail in picks rules block: Analyst may only name teammates appearing on the `Teammates (active/whitelisted)` line or in today's injury report; prohibits naming historical or absent teammates not present in today's context. |
| **lineup_update.py Comprehensive Overhaul (March 14, 2026)** | Fixed six failure modes causing the agent to silently skip on every real-world absence event. **F1 (root cause):** `compute_lineup_diff()` now uses TWO sources — snapshot starters AND picks.json. Any player with open picks today who is OUT/DOUBTFUL is now a `new_absence` regardless of snapshot state. Function signature extended with `today_picks`; picks loading moved before diff call in `main()`. **F2:** `build_opportunity_suggestions()` now runs an opponent scan for `defensive_anchor`/`rim_anchor` absences — finds whitelisted players on the opposing team; new `side="opponent"` field. **F4:** `classify_absent_player()` now falls back to picks.json when player not in player_stats — infers role_tags from pick_value (PTS≥20→high_usage, REB≥6→rim_anchor+defensive_anchor, AST≥4→primary_creator). **F5:** `--debug` flag added to main() — full diagnostic output without LLM call or file writes. **F3/F6:** Resolved as consequence of F1. Real-world trigger: Giannis OUT on 2026-03-14 — not in Rotowire snapshot starters, diff returned empty, Jalen Johnson opponent opportunity never surfaced. |
| **3PM Blowout Hard Skip + Parlay One-Player-Per-Card (March 14, 2026)** | **3PM blowout hard skip (`analyst.py`):** New rule added to KEY RULES — SEQUENTIAL GAME CONTEXT: when a player's 3PM trend is "down" AND BLOWOUT_RISK=True (favored team, spread_abs > 8), skip all 3PM picks including T1. Rule explicitly overrides [iron_floor]. New skip_reason key: `3pm_blowout_trend_down`. Motivated by: Donovan Mitchell 3PM T1 miss (2026-03-13) in a 33-point CLE blowout win where iron_floor provided no protection against game-script volume compression. **Parlay one-player-per-card (`parlay.py`):** Tightened concentration cap from max-2-parlays-per-player to max-1-parlay-per-player. Both `> 2` thresholds changed to `> 1` in `enforce_concentration_cap()`; `## AVOID` section in `build_parlay_prompt()` updated to match; docstring and log messages updated. Motivated by: Alperen Sengun appearing in 2 parlays on 2026-03-13 — single DNP caused both to miss simultaneously. |
| **Rotowire projected minutes — correct data source (March 12, 2026)** | Root cause: `parse_projected_minutes()` and `parse_onoff_usage()` were parsing `nba-lineups.php` HTML, which does not include premium panels in its server-rendered response. Diagnostic confirmed `/basketball/projected-minutes.php` is fully statically rendered and contains all target CSS classes (`lineups-viz`: 505, `minutes-meter__proj`: 439, `lineups-viz__player-name`: 145). `/basketball/projections.php?type=today` confirmed JS-rendered (0 tables, 0 player links despite 367K HTML). Fix: `ROTOWIRE_MINUTES_URL` constant added; `fetch_rotowire_minutes_html()` added; `main()` makes second authenticated fetch for the dedicated page and passes resulting soup to premium parsers. Health-check log added to `parse_projected_minutes()`: reports teams count + players-with-minutes-gt-0 count per run. First run with real projected minutes data expected next analyst cycle. |
